I also hope that you will report the actual situation of the existing teams and the concrete plans for research, organization, and transformation to the Headquarters for future reference, and that their effectiveness will be used for evaluation." Chiang himself is still in Hankou, and will probably go to Lushan within days. The rumor that he left Hankou on the 10th is completely untrue. (August 12th)

Central Standing Committee Revises Legislative Program 85

The Central Standing Committee of the Kuomintang passed the program for legislative procedures at its 25th meeting, and after revisions at its 28th Standing Committee meeting, sent it to the Central Political Council for review. The Central Political Council presented reports at its 316th and 318th meetings, and resolved to submit it to the National Government, which has examined the original document and instructed the Legislative Yuan to comply with it. The program is recorded as follows: (1) The agencies with the power to propose all legal bills and their proposals are as follows: 1. Cases submitted by the National Government to the Legislative Yuan for review; 2. Cases proposed by the Legislative Yuan itself; 3. Cases transferred by the Executive Yuan, the Judicial Yuan, the Examination Yuan, and the Control Yuan to the Legislative Yuan for review.

Page 11

Continued Important News

(2) Proposals for legal bills from various ministries and commissions of each Yuan should be submitted to their respective Yuan for approval, and then transferred by the respective Yuan to the Legislative Yuan. (3) The procedure for proposals for legal bills from provincial governments and municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan shall be the same as the method for proposals from various ministries and commissions. (4) For the submission of legal bills from agencies directly under the National Government other than the Five Yuans, they should all be submitted to the National Government for approval, and then submitted by the National Government to the Legislative Yuan for review. (5) For all legal bills, except for those proposed by the Political Council itself, which shall determine the principles themselves, those proposed by the proposing agencies listed in Article 1 shall be drafted by the original proposing agency and submitted to the Political Council for decision. The submitting agencies listed in Articles 2, 3, and 4 shall review and determine the draft principles of the legal bill and submit it to the Political Council for decision. The Legislative Yuan shall not change the principles set by the Political Council, but the Legislative Yuan may present its views to the Political Council. When each proposing agency submits a request to the Political Council for a decision on the principles, if there is already a full draft, it should be attached to the draft. (6) If the Central Political Council considers it necessary to amend a legal bill passed by the Legislative Yuan before it is promulgated by the National Government, it may issue the bill to the Legislative

Yuan to amend it accordingly.

Third Day of the Noulens Case Trial 86

Handwriting Expert States Opinion Four Times

The Noulens Deliberately Make Trouble, the Judge's Anger Is Visible

On the 12th, the third day of the Noulens case trial opened. Thirty to forty people were in attendance, and lawyer Chen Ying and Noulens' relatives, Feng Jiesi, were also present. At 8:55 AM, Judge Li Mian, Judge Lin Zhemian, Judge Yin Yuexu, Prosecutor Zhu Jun, Translator Chen Shidi, Clerk Wu Daquan, and others arrived. The bailiff brought up the documents, and then immediately signed to bring up the Noulens, Wang Deli, and Zeng Zhi. At 9:20 AM, Mr. Mason, a handwriting expert employed by the Shanghai Municipal Council, was also summoned to the court to state his opinion on handwriting analysis, proving that the handwriting on various documents was written by the Noulens and Wang Deli Zeng. The judge summoned Wang Deli Zeng and asked for his opinion on the expert report. Wang created trouble unreasonably, demanding that the court read out the original text of a letter that was not related to the handwriting analysis. The original text of the letter was in French. After the court read it out, Wang demanded that the Chinese translation be read, and then demanded that the English translation be read. All of this was unrelated to the handwriting analysis. The Noulens refused to answer any questions about the handwriting analysis, clearly showing their intention to cause trouble. The court hearing ended at 1 PM on the same day, and it was decided to continue the hearing on the 15th and summon witnesses Ross Moore, Pan A'da, Ding Zheng Sheng, and others. It is expected that this hearing will be one of the most important. The following is a record of the court hearing on the 12th. (Judge) First, Noulens was asked, "You deposited 1,500 US dollars in the Mei Feng Bank. The letter you wrote to the Mei Feng Bank was written by you personally. This letter was handed over by the representative of the Mei Feng Bank. There is also a letter that you wrote to the police station after you were arrested. This was also written by you yourself. Now I will show it to you." (The judge then handed Noulens the letter to the Mei Feng Bank for review.) (Noulens) "I request the letter to the police station to be shown." (Judge) "Your handwriting has been authenticated by the police station as being written by you. There is also Exhibit 18, which was typed. You made some changes on it. These words are the same as the letter you wrote to the Mei Feng Bank." (The judge immediately handed over Exhibit 18 to Noulens for detailed review.) (Noulens) "In this document, there is no evidence of communist activities or other crimes." (Judge) "I am only asking if you made these changes." (Noulens) "Please note that pages 136 and 137 of this document were not typed on the same typewriter." (Judge) "That doesn't matter. You just say whether this handwriting is yours." (Noulens) "I will not answer." (Judge) "Why don't you answer? Yesterday, when I asked you about the evidence in the iron box, you did not answer, saying that it was because the evidence of the crime was in the iron box. Now I am only asking you if you changed the handwriting." (Noulens) "I request that the results of the authentication be shown." At this point, the judge summoned the handwriting expert, Mr. Mason, to the court. The time was 9:30 AM. The judge first asked the expert for his name, origin, age, and profession. According to his testimony, his name was Mason, he was British, 24 years old, and worked in the fingerprint department of the Shanghai police station. He had specialized in the study of handwriting. The judge then informed him that he should truthfully state his authentication opinion and ordered him to sign a pledge, which he did one by one. At this time, the Noulens suddenly stood up and objected to Mr. Mason's testimony, saying that the police station's staff could not testify. The judge stopped them and then asked Mr. Mason, (Judge) "After the Noulens and Wang Deli Zeng were arrested in the Shanghai concession, did you authenticate their handwriting?" (Mason) "Yes." (Judge) "You said that the letter the Noulens wrote to the Mei Feng Bank was written by the Noulens personally. What is your opinion?" (Mason) "Here is an enlarged photograph of the letter the Noulens wrote to the Mei Feng Bank." (While speaking, he took out the photograph. The Noulens shouted loudly in opposition. The judge ordered them to maintain order. The Noulens were helpless and demanded that the expert state his opinion loudly so that they could hear it.) Mason continued, "There is also a photograph, which is an enlarged photograph of Exhibit 18 on page 139 of the first volume of the evidence book." (Judge) "How can you see that the handwriting is the same in these two enlarged photographs?" (Mason) "After careful examination, I found several points in common: (1) In the handwriting in both documents, every letter is written to the upper right. (2) In the handwriting in both documents, the letters are of inconsistent sizes. (3) The arrangement of the letters is also uneven and not in a straight line. (4) As far as the structure of the words is concerned, the lowercase "s" at the end of the word in both documents does not curve, but is slightly inclined straight down. (5) The lowercase "i" has two ways of writing: one is that it is not connected to the preceding letter or the following letter, and the other is that it is connected to the preceding letter but not connected to the following letter. (6) When the lowercase "ng" are connected together, the "N" is written straight, and the lower part of the "g" is biased to the left. (7) The uppercase "F" is written the same way in both documents. (8) The uppercase "M" is the same in the word "Manage" in the letter to the Mei Feng Bank and the "M" written in Exhibit 18. One curve on the left is at a higher angle than one curve on the right. (9) The "O" in both documents is connected to the preceding letter, and the top is open. The "O" in the words "Contents" in the Mei Feng Bank letter and "Conspiracy" in Exhibit 18 are both like this. (10) The lowercase "F" is first curved up, then straight down, and no longer curves back up. Based on these points in common, it is determined that the handwriting in these two documents was written by the same person." At this point, the judge summoned Noulens and asked, "What do you have to say about this?" (Noulens) "According to Article 24, paragraph 7, and Article 119 of the Criminal Procedure Law, I have the right to request the cancellation of this expert because he is a staff member of the police station." (Judge) "Don't misunderstand the articles. Article 24 of the Criminal Procedure Law states the reasons why a judge should recuse himself. Article 119 states that an expert can be rejected if he has the same reasons as a judge. Mr. Mason does not have this kind of reason now, so you cannot reject him." (Noulens) "According to Article 24 of the Criminal Procedure Law, he is a staff member of the police station and of course cannot be an expert." (Judge) "Incorrect. Article 24, paragraph 7, refers to a person who is a judge, an expert, and a prosecutor at the same time. Mr. Mason is not like this now, and this refers to the institution, not to a specific person." (Noulens) "On August 3rd of last year, at the Shanghai High Court No. 2 Branch, the presiding judge said that if we objected to the police station's expert, we could find another expert." (Judge) "You first said that Mr. Mason cannot be an expert. Now I have explained it to you, and you are changing the subject." (Noulens) "I have a few things I want to say now: (1) I am not surprised that a court without jurisdiction allows a person without qualifications to be an expert. (2) The search procedure was illegal because no list was made, so I can object to any staff member of the police station being an expert. (3) I request that the court find an expert who belongs to the court and also authenticates Exhibits 19, 23, 53, 56, 57, etc., which the government announced last year as having my handwriting. The handwriting in these documents is very difficult to authenticate. (4) In addition to the documents published in the Continental Daily on September 16th of last year, it was also said that Exhibits 38, 47, 49, 51, 52, 54, 55, etc., also have my handwriting. I request that they also be authenticated together. (5) I request that this police station's expert be cancelled." (Judge) "All of these words are incorrect. First, regarding the issue of jurisdiction, the Supreme Court has repeatedly rejected your application, and this court of course has jurisdiction. Second, you said that police station staff cannot be experts because the police station's search was illegal, but according to the Shanghai court's agreement, the police station has the right to search, and the Shanghai court also has search warrants. Moreover, this expert is authenticating based on his knowledge and has nothing to do with the institution. Third, experts are specialized talents. In countries around the world, these experts are attached to institutions, otherwise it would not be easy to find them. For example, fingerprinters are attached to the police department. If the court asks him to authenticate, how can you say that he is illegal? Fourth, if you attack the expert's authentication as being incorrect, that is acceptable, but you cannot say that he is the wrong person. Fifth, your request to hire another expert is contradictory. On the one hand, you say that this court has no jurisdiction, and on the other hand, you ask this court to hire another expert. Aren't you contradicting yourself? Sixth, now this court is first authenticating this document. As for whether or not to authenticate the documents published in the Continental Daily, that is another matter, and this court has the right to decide." (Noulens) "I still have to state that: (1) The opinions that I have expressed that are favorable to me have not been recognized by the court. (2) After this case occurred, the Supreme Court of China and this court have stated that they would handle it with caution, but there are many facts in the indictment that have no evidence, and they have actually been given the crime of death. (3) The court and the prosecutor have never given us a chance to prove our innocence. (4) The issue of jurisdiction is not based on the law. We are being tried here under duress, and the court is not allowing us to make an appropriate defense. (5) We are not now authorizing the lawyers to defend us in this court. We requested the court yesterday not to allow the lawyers to defend us in this court, but to still allow them to record in this court. We are not afraid of being tried in any Chinese court, but the court must be based on Chinese law." (At this point, the judge said that if they were not authorizing the lawyers, they could withdraw them. Noulens said that it was not that they were dissatisfied with lawyer Chen, but that they did not want to defend in this court. The judge then showed them the letter of authorization and ordered them not to waffle, but to focus on the authentication.) (6) The government authorities have published the documents in this case, but the defense lawyers are not allowed to photograph the documents when they request to do so. (7) In Europe, defendants have the right to find independent experts. (8) According to Chinese law, I have the right to object to the expert. (9) As far as I know, this expert has never appeared in court before. (10) The person who cracked this case is still police chief Givens of the police station, who is Mason's superior. If Mason is the expert, he will not be fair. (10) (1) To authenticate handwriting, you can find people from banks or stores. They have more research in comparison. We have been detained for 14 months, and the court has the responsibility to find them. (Judge) "Your reasons for rejecting this expert are not valid. I have already said that I will not answer your attack on his identity. You should express your opinion on his authentication opinion." (Noulens) "According to Article 299 of the Criminal Procedure Law, I request that the court make a ruling on rejecting my objection to the expert." (Judge) "I have already made a verbal ruling. Now you answer his authentication opinion. If you do not answer, you will be at a disadvantage." (At this point, the judge ordered Mr. Mason to repeat his authentication opinion to Noulens. Noulens refused to answer.) (To be continued)

Talk by Yu Tan, Director of the Railway Department 87

Implementing Responsible Transportation on All National Railways; Nanjing Correspondence: Recently, the Ministry of Railways is reorganizing the national railway administration. The first new measure they are undertaking is to implement responsible transportation on all railways. To understand the nature of this measure, we specially visited Yu Tan, Director of the Railway Department, who informed us of the details of the matter. The conversation is as follows: (Reporter asks) What is responsible transportation? (Answer) For example, when transporting goods by railway, from the time the owner delivers the goods to the station and requests transportation, to the time the railway transports the goods to the destination station and delivers them to the consignee, if the goods are lost during railway transportation or storage, the railway is responsible for compensation at the assessed value, except for force majeure events such as natural disasters or human calamities. Moreover, the goods can be transported to the destination station within the scheduled time without delay. This is what is called responsible transportation of goods. All European and American countries have adopted this system. In our country, only the Jiaoji and Beining lines have trialed it. (Question) What is the current method of goods transportation? (Answer) At present, Chinese railways generally use a method of irresponsible transportation. Merchants entrust goods for transportation, but they are often not transported for months, resulting in spoilage or theft. Even if they are transported, theft during the journey and collisions during loading and unloading cause significant losses to merchants. Merchants, whose capital is at stake, often view railway transportation as a dangerous path and turn to water transportation. As a result, forwarding companies have emerged. Forwarding companies operate by transporting goods on behalf of customers and earning a small commission. If managed properly, they can coexist with the railways without conflict. However, the current forwarding companies take advantage of the railways' irresponsible transportation, monopolize the market, and engage in deception and fraud against customers. For example, if a merchant has goods and wants to transport them by railway, directly entrusting them to the railway may result in indefinite delays and potential losses. They believe that having a forwarding company send an escort can prevent losses. However, forwarding companies intentionally create scarcity and demand exorbitant fees, with transportation costs often several times higher than the railway's original rates. Merchants who want to avoid unexpected losses and ensure speedy delivery have no choice but to spend heavily to satisfy their demands. As for goods of lower value, merchants cannot bear the losses of railway transportation and the exorbitant demands of forwarding companies, and would rather have them pile up in the production area than transport them out, leading to the current national economic distress. Railway freight has declined, the business community is in panic, and the national economy and people's livelihood are directly and negatively affected, while forwarding companies alone enjoy huge profits. This current method of railway transportation urgently needs improvement. (Question) Is there a solid guarantee that responsible transportation will be effective for the railways? (Answer) Implementing responsible transportation can reverse the current chronic problems of railway freight, as mentioned above. As for its effectiveness, let the performance of the Beining Railway serve as proof. In 1928, to attract freight, the Beining Railway cooperated with the Sitao and other railways for intermodal transportation. However, because Beining was not responsible for freight at the time, 99% of the goods transported from the Sitao and other railways were still absorbed by the South Manchuria Railway. By the end of 1930, Beining announced the implementation of responsible freight transportation. On that very day, more than 600 carloads of goods that had already been entrusted to the South Manchuria Railway were temporarily switched to the Beining Railway. And the Beining Railway, excluding the period after the September 18th Incident last year, increased its revenue by 3.3 million yuan in just nine months from the eleven stations with responsible transportation. The initial implementation has been so effective. If all the national railways follow suit, the results can be imagined in due course. (Question) How will the implementation of responsible transportation affect existing forwarding companies? (Answer) The original meaning of forwarding companies is to complement the railways. If forwarding companies can attract freight for the railways, the railways will have no reason to discriminate against them. However, forwarding companies arbitrarily exploit customers, causing freight to be impeded, and the railways are indirectly harmed by this. Therefore, the railways have to devise self-help strategies. Implementing responsible transportation is one such strategy. If forwarding companies can adopt a low-profit approach in the future, transporting goods on behalf of customers and earning only a small commission without making excessive demands, then railway freight will inevitably become prosperous. In the minds of cargo owners, as long as forwarding companies handle the transportation, various procedures can be avoided, and small expenses are acceptable. Forwarding companies should take advantage of this psychology and reduce commissions, so that their business will flourish even more. There is no need to be unduly concerned about the railway implementing responsible freight transportation. Finally, Director Yu also said that the beneficiaries of the railway's implementation of responsible transportation are not only the railways, freight merchants, and forwarding companies, but also the people's livelihood and economy. The flow of goods and corresponding supply will prevent the national livelihood from being as impoverished as it is today. Moreover, merchants who entrust goods for transportation and obtain a bill of lading issued by the railway can use this bill of lading as collateral to obtain loans from banks because the railway is responsible for it, allowing capital to circulate and stimulating the business community. Therefore, the implementation of responsible transportation is entirely beneficial and without any drawbacks. I hope to use the power of the newspapers to promote this innovative measure of the railway authorities and gain the sympathy of the public.

Local Correspondence

Taicang 88

Director Dong of the Construction Department Inspects Dangers in Taicang. The sea dikes at Liuhe Estuary, Daotang Temple, Parade Ground, Yanglinkou, and other places in the county were impacted by strong winds and storm surges the day before, and the dikes were on the verge of collapse, posing an extremely dangerous situation. Qiu Xijue, Director of the Construction Bureau of Taicang County and concurrently Director of the Dike Works, immediately telegraphed the provincial department to report the dangerous situation. Dong Xiujia, Director of the Construction Department, arrived in Taicang at 8:00 AM yesterday and, together with Zhao Enju, the county magistrate, and Qiu Xijue, Director of the Dike Works, went to the dangerous areas to conduct an on-site inspection. Director Dong believed that the section of the dike was extremely dangerous. If it was not repaired quickly, the entire Taicang County would become a swamp once it collapsed, which was a matter of great importance to the safety of the area. He immediately approved the engineering estimate and ordered active repairs. The inspection was completed around 2:00 PM before he returned to Taicang.

Songjiang 89

Requesting Funds for Emergency Repairs on the Second Section of the Sea Dike. In addition to the third and fourth sections of the Songjiang Sea Dike Post-Disaster Project, which have been completed as scheduled, Xu Baikui, Director of the Jiangnan Sea Dike Songjiang Section Engineering Office, has also prepared budgets for the emergency repairs of other sections, explaining the extent of the dangers and submitting them to the Dike Works Committee and the Construction Department for funding requests. It is reported that the second section of the dike is the most dangerous, as no post-disaster work has been carried out since the danger occurred last year. Not only have the wood pilings rotted, but the dike foundation has also been washed away in several places. In addition, there are no large stones in the middle of the old dike in this section. In the event of a sudden storm surge, the danger is extremely worrying. Therefore, more than ten zhang of dike soil was washed away during the strong wind the night before. Su, Director of the Construction Department, also visited Songjiang to inspect and recognized the importance of the section's engineering. According to the Type A wood-stone engineering plan prepared by the office, the cost of labor and materials requires 77,792 yuan. Director Xu has reported this to the Construction Department and consulted with the Jiangnan Dike Works Committee, requesting the prompt issuance of funds to prepare for construction as soon as possible to prevent unforeseen events. This matter concerns the lives of the people of Songyi, and everyone hopes for repairs to begin as soon as possible.

Suzhou 90

Situation of the Nine-County Joint Defense Conference. The last issue of this newspaper briefly reported that the Wu-Kun-Jiang-Qing and other nine-county joint defense conference held its third meeting in Kunshan on the 12th. It is now known that the meeting was chaired by Zou Jing, the magistrate of Wu County, and the following resolutions were made: (1) The public security bureaus and district offices of each county are responsible for re-checking the population registration; (2) The methods for dealing with roving bandits and disbanded soldiers in each county are stipulated; (3) The fourth meeting will be held in Songjiang on September 9th. Magistrate Zou and others have already returned to Suzhou.

Bandits from Pudong Flee to Zhejiang. Since the summer and autumn, various gangs of river bandits have been plotting uprisings. Although the water police have repeatedly suppressed them, these bandits scatter and gather, making it difficult to eliminate them. Recently, about 300 river bandits from Pudong, divided into more than 20 bandit boats, fled from Dianshan Lake to Wusong Port and sneaked into Zhejiang Province. Shen, the district chief of the third water police district, reported the above to the commander and ordered the Zhenwei two patrol ships to join the fourteenth and fifteenth teams to head to Wusong Port for interception on the 13th.

Xu Yabo Case Scheduled for Sentencing. Xu Yabo, the former chief of the first water police district, who refused to accept the first-instance verdict in the case of conspiracy and robbery, appealed to the High Court. Yesterday was the continuation of the trial. The court session was held in the third criminal court at 10:00 AM. Judge Song Yuan and prosecutor Wang Shicheng were present. Only witness Pan Guangxi reported, and all other witnesses were absent. After a long investigation, Xu Yabo claimed to be falsely accused. Subsequently, Xu's lawyers Chen Zhengmin, Fei Tinghuang, and Xu Helin stood up to defend him successively. After the prosecutor's statement, the court ordered the debate to end and scheduled the sentencing for 8:00 AM on the 18th. Xu was still remanded in custody.

Faculty and Students of Soochow University Aid Volunteer Army. In view of the fact that volunteer armies in Northeast China were fighting bravely in the battlefield under the scorching sun, the faculty and students of Soochow University in Suzhou initiated an on-campus fundraising campaign to provide material support to the volunteer army. Faculty, staff, and students actively donated. Other schools are also in the process of organizing.

Wujiang 91

Tax Inspectors Illegally Detained. Xie and Gao, two inspectors from the county's stamp tax bureau, went to Zhenze in the county to check store stamps the day before. On the spot, they seized 65 books of records. Inspector Xie arbitrarily imposed a fine of 95 yuan. Xu Ziyi, chairman of the Zhenze District Chamber of Commerce, learned that the inspectors dared to impose fines privately, which violated the stamp tax trial regulations. He immediately telegraphed the local public security bureau to detain them temporarily for transfer to the county for legal action. After the stamp tax bureau received the news, it immediately sent Yu Boliang to mediate. The inspectors have been temporarily released on bail.

Wuxi 92

County Bureau Issues Proclamation on Levying Business Tax. Since the implementation of the business tax in Jiangsu Province, disputes have arisen repeatedly. Recently, the newly revised provisional regulations on business tax have been issued, and the tax rates have been revised, ordering all counties to uniformly levy taxes in the autumn of this year. However, chambers of commerce in various places have repeatedly requested a reduction in tax rates. The Wuxi County Government and the Business Tax Collection Bureau jointly issued a proclamation yesterday, ordering uniform compliance with the tax levy. The original text reads roughly as follows: "Having examined the newly revised provisional regulations on business tax and the revised tax rates, we are ordered to comply with and implement them. Therefore, starting from the autumn of this year, whether wholesale or retail, all taxes will be levied according to the newly set tax rates and classifications. All taxes not paid in the autumn and winter of last year and the spring of this year will still be paid directly to the bureau in full within 20 days according to the old tax rates for reporting and submission. At the same time, those who have not yet filled out and submitted declaration forms must truthfully fill them out and submit them to the bureau within five days for review and tax levy. If they continue to refuse to declare, or refuse investigation, or make false declarations, or attempt to evade taxes, conceal books, or forge accounts and certificates, the director of this office will strictly enforce the law and severely punish them."

Jiangyin 93

Director of the Public Security Sub-bureau Dismissed. Li Mutang, director of the second branch of the Qingyang Public Security Bureau, was stripped of his position as the head of the first branch of the bureau for the case where he was dragged to the head bureau for parading by a patrol officer, Li Chunshan, and others. Zhang Fengqing was dispatched by the provincial government to Chengdiao to investigate. Li was scheduled to be summoned for questioning on the 10th, but when a call was made to Qingyang, Li Mutang had already left for Xixi due to a guilty conscience. Liu Hanzhen, the bureau director, dismissed Li on the 11th for leaving his post without permission and disregarding official orders.

Villagers in the Eighth District Expel the District Chief. Recently, in Zhouzhuang Town in the eighth district, a drought and epidemic have broken out, first in the rural areas and then in the markets. The rural areas are scattered and increasingly widespread, and deaths have followed one another. Local people in the township were confused by superstition and pooled money to hire Taoist priests to build a Taiping Gong Jiao ceremony. Yesterday (the 12th), they wanted to borrow the Eighth District Office as a Taoist ritual site for four days. Xu Lianqu, the district chief, refused. Hundreds of people gathered and shouted to expel the district chief. Xu, seeing that the situation was unfavorable, fled to the city and stayed at the Huayuan Hotel. Soon, Miao Lunqian and Chen Zhongda, fearing that the matter would escalate, tried their best to mediate and allowed the district office to be borrowed as a Taoist ritual site, and peace was restored.

County Representatives' Assembly Scheduled to Resume. The fourth session of the County Representatives' Assembly, which lasted for three days and was extended for one day, was adjourned on the 8th due to difficulties in electing executive and supervisory committee members and insufficient quorum. Wang Zhenxian, the election supervisor, and Xi Hanping, a standing member of the county executive committee, personally presented the matter to the provincial government. On the 12th, the provincial executive committee decided to resume the meeting on the 24th to elect executive and supervisory committee members, and Wang Zhenxian was still appointed as the election supervisor.

Nantong 94

All Public Security Sub-bureaus in the Four Rural Districts Abolished. Because there are no fixed funds and the daily measures are unpopular, all public security sub-bureaus and branch offices in the four rural districts of Nantong, totaling more than 20, were abolished according to a resolution passed at the county administrative meeting on the 12th. All security will be the responsibility of the defense corps. According to the interpretation of the Ministry of Internal Affairs, public security administration will be handled by the district offices. However, in prosperous cities and towns, those that must be established for commercial purposes must have more than 1,000 merchants and a local monthly business donation income of more than 240 yuan before they can apply for approval to establish a sub-bureau or branch office. The jurisdiction is limited to the city or town. The police officers in each abolished sub-bureau and branch office will be issued retirement certificates by the county public security bureau. After assessment, they may be given priority for supplemental recruitment in the county public security bureau, county police team, and district defense corps.

Wangjia Temple Bandit Robbery Case: Criminal Executed by Shooting. In the Wangjia Temple bandit robbery case in Tangzha District, the two criminals Li Jinbiao and Xu Zhen, who were caught on the spot, were brought to the county government together with the weapons they had seized for interrogation. They were sentenced to death. Magistrate Zhang presented the case to the provincial government for approval. On the 12th, an electric reply was received approving the execution by shooting at the scene of the crime.

The first battalion of the first regiment of the Jiangsu Provincial Security Team infantry, led by Gao Zhiwen, departed from Tong on the 9th and arrived in Rugao. It is planned to send one company to station in Shizhuang and one company to station in Xixiang. The battalion headquarters is located in the Jile Temple in the city.

Yi Ruichang Sues Wang Yuanchen Again. They sued each other, and the case was widely reported in the provincial capital. Recently, Wang claimed that Yi's illness was incurable (and he had been hospitalized for nearly two years, paying 100 yuan in medical expenses. According to the settlement, medical expenses and other fees amounted to more than 1,900 yuan). Moreover, the Provincial Hospital is publicly established and cannot afford the expenses, so Yi was carried to the Jiangsheng Newspaper and returned to the introducer. On that day, Wang took two weeks of leave to go to Lushan for summer vacation and was scheduled to return to Zhenjiang around the 16th. During this period, Huang Shengbai was responsible for the hospital affairs. However, Yi sued Wang in court for abandonment. Wang was unable to attend the court session the other day because he was not in Zhenjiang. It is now heard that the hearing has been rescheduled.

Investigating Guo Zhaobi, the Swallowing Relief District Chief of the Seventh District. During last year's flood, most of the spring relief distributed in each district was embezzled. Cases of district and town chiefs being accused of embezzling relief funds have emerged repeatedly. Jiaxing 98

Construction Bureau Abolished and Converted into a Section. The Jiaxing County Construction Bureau has been ordered to be abolished and converted into a Construction Section. After receiving the order, Director Liang immediately began to wind up the affairs. The bureau has been abolished the day before and converted into a Construction Section of the County Government. Director Liang Hua has been reassigned as the section chief and receives his original salary. However, the funding has been reduced to 256 yuan compared to before. Therefore, some of the old staff will be laid off, and the salaries of those who remain will also need to be reduced. For the convenience of handling affairs, it is still necessary to divide it into several units.

Ningbo 99

Fan Chun Guan Detained. Fan Chun Guan, a businessman in Ningbo, is the chairman of the Ningbo Rice Industry Association and the manager of Tian Feng Yihe Rice Shop. His eldest son, Fan Weichen, is the director of the collection office of the Yin County Government. Fan Chun Guan used more than 50,000 yuan of public funds from the county government collection office due to speculative failures in the rice industry. Tianfeng and other rice shops also went bankrupt as a result. The county government discovered the matter and summoned Fan Chun Guan to the government for negotiations. After Fan used houses and other properties as collateral, there was still a shortage of more than 30,000 yuan. The county government requested instructions from the province, and the province ordered that he must be detained. Therefore, Fan Chun Guan was detained yesterday afternoon.

Draft National Physical Education Implementation Plan (1) 103

The National Physical Education Implementation Plan was drafted by Messrs. Wu Yunrui, Yuan Dunli, and Hao Gengsheng at the request of the National Physical Education Conference Preparatory Committee. It will be submitted to the conference for discussion. The draft is recorded as follows:

｜Table of Contents｜ I. Introduction, II. Objectives, III. Administration and Facilities, (I) Administrative and Organizational System, (II) Equipment, (III) Funding, IV. Methods for Promoting Physical Education, (I) Research Work, (II) Training of Personnel, (III) Standards for the Implementation of Physical Education, (IV) Promoting and Rewarding Various Physical Education Gatherings and Organizations, (V) Methods for Evaluating Physical Education, V. Phased Implementation Plan

(I) Introduction: To solve a problem, one must first understand the meaning and scope of the problem itself, and then discuss solutions. The meaning of the term "physical education" varies greatly in different eras and societies, and people generally have different understandings of physical education. If its meaning is not clarified and its scope defined first, and an implementation plan is hastily stipulated, it will not only be difficult to know where to start, but even after implementation, it is likely that the result will deviate from the original intention, which is extremely dangerous. Therefore, before drafting this plan, the meaning and scope of physical education must be briefly stated. In the eyes of ordinary people, physical education is nothing more than physical exercise. However, since the development of biology and psychology, the traditional dualistic theory of mind and body has ceased to exist, and the purpose of modern education is not only to provide knowledge, but also to train the entire organism for life. Therefore, we have come to deeply understand that although physical education appears to be large muscle activity, it causes many physiological and psychological changes, and it is an indispensable method for training the entire organism for life. Therefore, the meaning of physical education is not only physical exercise, but also providing educational opportunities through various large muscle activities of the body. In other words, to achieve various educational goals, physical activity is a major means and method. The development and health promotion of the organism is a natural result of physical activity. Physical education not only achieves this goal, but also has other important educational goals, such as social morality, basic life skills, methods for making good use of leisure time, and the attitudes and abilities that citizens must possess, all of which can be trained and cultivated through various physical activities. Therefore, physical education and education cannot be separated into two. The only difference is that physical education uses large muscle activity of the body as a method to achieve educational goals, while education uses other methods in addition to physical education to achieve its goals. Therefore, all physical education facilities must be based on the standard of being able to achieve the entire educational purpose. At the same time, anything that does not use large muscle activity of the body as an educational method cannot be called physical education. For the sake of a clear understanding of the scope of physical education, the following points must be explained here:

(I) Physical Education and Military Training: The purpose of military training is to provide citizens with military knowledge, train citizens' ability to defend against insults, and cultivate citizens' national consciousness. The current military training in schools at all levels focuses on infantry drills, and because the training is not strict enough, not only is it difficult to achieve the true purpose of military training, but even soldiers who blindly obey orders and are not afraid of death cannot be obtained. To achieve the purpose of military training, on the one hand, it is necessary to strive for the development of science and industry, and the stability and consolidation of society and the economy. On the other hand, in addition to providing citizens with strict and thorough training in military life at a considerable age, it is necessary to cultivate national consciousness and the ability to defend against insults in many invisible ways. All subjects in schools must take this as their purpose, especially history, geography, and civics, which are the most effective. As for physical education, it provides citizens with fully developed bodies and brave and agile spirits, which contributes greatly to achieving the purpose of military training invisibly. It goes without saying that if infantry drills are regarded as physical education and used as the main method of military national training, then what could be more absurd? Therefore, in addition to the inherent value of physical education, which indirectly contributes to military training, the government has other methods for all aspects of military training, and there is no need to involve it.

(II) Physical Education and Hygiene and Health Education: Because physical education can promote development and health, it is often regarded as a part of hygiene, or hygiene as a part of physical education. In fact, the two have their own scope and cannot be mixed into one. From a social perspective, hygiene is one of the important functions of the government, including the supply of medicine, the improvement of the environment, the prevention of diseases, and the facilities for public health training and guidance. From a school perspective, health is one of the most important goals of education, including health protection and inspection, environmental hygiene facilities, and the establishment of appropriate health education. Health is an element of life, and education must be related to actual life. All activities and facilities in schools must have the meaning and components of health education. Since physical education is one of the subjects and activities in schools, it naturally makes a considerable contribution to health education. It has been said before that the inevitable result of physical education is to promote the development and health of the organism. This is its greatest contribution to health education. However, in addition to this inevitable health result, physical education has other major contributions to education. Moreover, the constituent elements of physical education are purely large muscle activities, while the constituent elements of health education are contained in all school activities and teaching. Therefore, although physical education and health education both belong to the scope of education, there is actually a great difference between them. This plan can only be based on the scope of physical education and does not involve hygiene and health education.

(III) Physical Education and Labor: Since physical education is the activity of large muscles, it is often considered similar to labor. Some even advocate replacing physical education with labor. However, the purpose and meaning of the two are different. The purpose of labor is production, and the purpose of physical education is education. Labor is sometimes harmful to the body of children, so it is not suitable for underage children to work. This has long been recognized by sociologists and educators. Physical education is the only tool for developing the body and mind. If productive labor is used to replace children's games and sports, there is nothing more depriving of children's opportunities for development and education. Labor is the work of adults, and physical education is entertainment. Work is necessary for life, and appropriate entertainment is also indispensable for life. Moreover, the various educational goals that physical education wants to achieve, as mentioned above, cannot be achieved by labor. Therefore, those who advocate replacing physical education with labor are too trusting in utilitarianism and neglecting the various educational meanings within physical education.

(IV) Physical Education and Boy Scouts: The Boy Scouts were originally designed to train young people in the skills of serving as scouts in wartime. It has gradually developed into an organized and multi-faceted youth training program. Its main content is to provide young people with opportunities to contact nature and the actual society, so as to cultivate various life skills and proper attitudes towards people and things. Its organization method is purely extracurricular activities in schools. Thus, what is learned in the school classroom is practiced in this extracurricular design. Therefore, the Boy Scouts are actually an entire educational design, reaching their own special goals. Physical education cannot replace the Boy Scouts, just as the Boy Scouts cannot replace physical education. As for the various physical activities and skill tests practiced by the Boy Scouts, they are certainly not unrelated to physical education. Because it is an entire educational design, it is natural to adopt many physical education activities and materials. However, it goes without saying that this kind of physical education activities and materials should have considerable contact with the school's physical education curriculum.

(V) The Status of National Martial Arts in Physical Education: National martial arts are a unique physical activity method of our nation. On the one hand, it can provide self-defense skills, and on the other hand, it can be used as a tool for physical exercise. It not only has its fixed value in national history, but it is also not unscientific when observed from the perspective of modern science such as anatomy and physiology. Promoting and researching it is a necessity today. However, learning has no national boundaries, and human nature is the same regardless of origin. All kinds of physical education activities that do not violate scientific principles and can suit human nature should be promoted equally according to the domestic social situation. There should be no distinction based on the location of their origin. Therefore, national martial arts are actually a kind of physical education activity and should not be given a special status because they are unique to our country, so as to abandon other physical education activities that are in line with science and education. On the other hand, since learning has no national boundaries, our country's national martial arts should strive for its development in the international arena and should not regard it as a rare commodity to be hoarded. Looking at Japanese judo, it has recently been learned by many people in Europe and the United States, let alone the profundity of our country's national martial arts, which is far above it? As for domestic physical education experts, they should pay close attention to and study national martial arts deeply, while national martial artists should also have a considerable understanding of modern physical education and its basic subjects. This is the necessary path for developing and researching national martial arts.

(II) Objectives (I) Provide citizens with opportunities for full physical development, (II) Train citizens' ability to use their bodies flexibly to adapt to the environment, (III) Cultivate citizens' spirit of cooperation and solidarity, (IV) Cultivate citizens' style of chivalry and bravery, (V) Cultivate citizens' habit of using sports and games for entertainment.

(III) Administration and Facilities (I) Administrative and Organizational System: In China, in addition to the Department of Social Affairs of the Ministry of Education being in charge of mass sports, there are no other fixed administrative organs in the central administration of physical education. As a result, various physical education facilities lack a systematic plan and it is difficult to have good results. Although the National Physical Education Law has been promulgated by the Legislative Yuan, it has not been implemented to this day. Regardless of whether it is appropriate or not, it is equivalent to a dead letter. Based on the above-mentioned meaning and scope of physical education, and with reference to the organization of China's central administration, it is necessary today to establish a physical education committee within the Ministry of Education to manage all physical education administration in the country. All central administrative matters related to physical education must be passed by this committee to be effective, so that national physical education can be developed as a whole, consistently, and in a planned manner. However, the committee must be organized by recruiting outstanding physical education experts from all over the country. It cannot be stationed in Beijing all the time. It can only have regular gatherings. Therefore, there must be someone who is stationed in the Ministry of Education to implement the resolutions of the committee. Therefore, a physical education supervisor must be established in the Ministry of Education to take charge of this position. As for the Central Mass Sports Field, according to reason, it should be under the jurisdiction of the Department of Social Affairs of the Ministry of Education and should be handed over immediately in order to seek the unity of things. The draft outline of the committee's organization and the table of the central administrative system are listed below:

Draft Outline of the Organization of the Physical Education Committee 104

Article 1: The Ministry of Education of the National Government, in order to unify the national physical education administration and promote the development of national physical education, has specially established the Physical Education Committee to be responsible for planning, guiding, supervising, and reviewing the national physical education. Article 2: The number of members of this committee shall be ○ to ○. They shall be appointed by the Minister of Education from ○ people from the General Training Supervision Department, ○ people from the National Martial Arts Hall, and ○ physical education experts. The Minister of Education, the Vice Minister, the Director of the Department of Social Affairs, the Physical Education Supervisor of the Ministry of Education, and the Director of the Central Mass Sports Field shall be ex officio members. Article 3: This committee shall have ○ to ○ standing committee members, who shall be appointed by the Minister of Education from among the members. The Physical Education Supervisor of the Ministry of Education shall be an ex officio standing committee member. Article 4: This committee may establish a secretary when necessary to handle records and documents, who shall be appointed by the Minister of Education from the Secretariat. Article 5: The functions of this committee are as follows: (I) Planning national physical education facilities, (II) Guiding national physical education research and administration, (III) Supervising administrative organs at all levels to implement physical education plans, (IV) Reviewing, A. Physical education courses and grades of schools at all levels, B. Organizational plans and reports of various physical education institutions, C. Qualifications of physical education workers, (V) Preparing and reviewing the national physical education budget, (VI) Discussing matters referred by the Minister of Education. Article 6: The functions of the standing committee members are as follows: (I) Matters concerning the convening of meetings, (II) Matters concerning the implementation of resolutions. Article 7: This committee shall hold two general meetings each year, in February and August. The Standing Committee shall meet once a month. If there are special matters, extraordinary general meetings or extraordinary standing committee meetings may be held. Article 8: The term of office of the members appointed by this committee shall be one year, and they may be reappointed upon expiration. Article 9: This committee may convene the physical education supervisors of the education departments of various provinces, special municipalities, and ordinary cities to participate in meetings when necessary. Article 10: All members of this committee shall be honorary positions, but they may receive transportation expenses or travel expenses for attending meetings, working, or being sent out. Article 11: The detailed rules of procedure of this committee shall be determined separately. Article 12: The resolutions of this committee shall be submitted to the Minister of Education for approval and then handed over to the standing committee members, the physical education supervisor of the Ministry of Education, the physical education supervisors of the education departments and education bureaus of various provinces, and other competent authorities related to physical education for implementation. Article 13: If there are any matters not covered in this organizational outline, they may be amended by the proposal of the General Assembly with the consent of the Minister of Education. Article 14: This organizational outline shall be implemented from the date of approval by the Minister of Education.

Wang Jingwei Returned to His Residence Yesterday and Met with He, Song, and Zhu 109

But Wang's Attitude Was Resolute, and He Refused to Withdraw His Resignation

The Representatives Then Separately Reported to the Central Government and Chiang

Tang Youren Returned to Shanghai Yesterday After Reporting in Nanjing; The Central Government Emphasizes Chairman Chiang's Opinion Regarding the Resignation of Executive Yuan President Wang Jingwei and Is Still Exerting Utmost Efforts to Retain Him. However, for Days, Representatives from Various Parties, Except for One Formal Meeting with Wang on the Third Day After His Arrival in Shanghai, Have Been Received by Madam Wang. Until Yesterday, Three Representatives, Song Ziwen, He Yingqin, and Zhu Peide, Had Their Second Meeting with Wang. According to Discussions, Wang's Resignation Intention Has Not Been Dismissed, but He Is Considered a Courageous and Responsible Person, and an Appropriate Solution Will Be Found Soon.

Second Meeting to Persuade Wang to Stay: For Days, the Central Government, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, He Yingqin, Song Ziwen, and Song Peide Negotiated with Madam Chen Bijun, Wang Jingwei's Wife. After Madam Wang Conveyed He, Song, and Others' Intentions to Wang Himself, Wang Seemed Slightly Moved, and They Agreed to a Second Formal Meeting Yesterday Afternoon. In the Afternoon, Wang First Returned to His Residence on Rue Bourgeat at 12:35 PM to Wait. Song, He, and Zhu Then Arrived at Wang's Residence Together at 2:20 PM to Visit Wang. Madam Chen Bijun Was Also Present. The Three Representatives Sincerely Urged Wang to Stay Again and Requested Him to Go to Nanjing Soon to Resume His Duties. Wang's Attitude Remained Resolute, Believing That His Resignation Was the Best Way to Eliminate Irresponsible Military Personnel. Therefore, He Was Determined to Sacrifice His Personal Position to Achieve Military Unification. After Song and Others Repeatedly Urged Him to Resume His Position, Wang Finally Refused to Withdraw His Resignation. Finally, the Representatives Asked Wang to Give Serious Consideration to the Hopes of the Central Government and Chairman Chiang, but the Meeting Ended Without Result Around 4:00 PM.

Separate Letters to Nanjing and Hankou: Song, He, and Zhu Left Wang's Residence and Went to Song's Residence on Qiqi Road to Consult. They Decided to Report the Situation of the Meeting with Wang Separately to the Central Government and Chairman Chiang Kai-shek in Hankou and to Exchange Ideas on How to Persuade Wang to Stay. They Dispersed at 4:45 PM.

Representatives from All Parties Exerted Utmost Efforts to Persuade Wang to Stay. Wang Has Not Yet Expressed Any Intention to Dismiss His Resignation. However, Mr. Wang Is a Courageous and Responsible Person. I (He Himself) Believe That There Will Be a Reasonable Solution in the Next Few Days. As for the Premature Convocation of the Third Plenary Session, I Have Not Heard of It. I Don't Think Such a Move Will Occur. As for Returning to Nanjing, It Is Unlikely to Happen in the Next Day or Two.

Flying Arrows Were Tested Yesterday 110

Invented by Huang Tingyu of Northeast China

The Garrison Command Also Sent Personnel to Monitor Huang Tingyu, Who Served in the Northeast Army for Many Years, Is Enthusiastic About National Affairs, and Has Recently Invented a Flying Arrow After Repeated Research. It Is Specifically for Aerial Defense. He Previously Conducted an Experiment in Beiping, and the Altitude Reached 5,000 Meters, Which Was Highly Praised by Zhou Dawen, the Mayor of Beiping. He Recently Came to Shanghai and Reached an Agreement with the Garrison Command. Yesterday Afternoon at 2:00 PM, He Conducted a Live Test at the Longhua Airfield, Open to Public Viewing. The Garrison Command Also Sent Personnel to Monitor. Huang First Explained the Internal Structure of the Flying Arrow in Detail. The Arrow Is Several Feet Long, with the Top Filled with Explosives and the Tail in a Triangular Shape. Huang and His Assistants Then Placed the Flying Arrow in a Circular Iron Tube and Ignited the Fuse. With a Loud Boom, the Flying Arrow Soared into the Sky and Exploded in the Air. However, the Explosive Force Was Not Great. The First Two Arrows Only Reached Several Hundred Meters, and the Last One Reached More Than a Thousand Meters. In Fact, Its Effectiveness in Bombarding Aircraft Is Still Limited. However, Huang's Spirit and Perseverance Are Admirable. When a Reporter Asked Huang About This, He Said That He Would Continue to Work Hard to Meet the Expectations of the People. He Also Said That When Bombarding Aircraft in Actual Combat, a Protractor Should Be Prepared to Measure the Area of the Flying Arrow's Explosive Force in the Air, Which Is About 50 Meters.

Educational Associations of All Districts of This City Telegraph the League of Nations Investigation Team to Uphold Justice 112

Recently, the Educational Associations of All Districts of This City, in Light of Japan's Seizure of Customs Posts and Intrusion into Rehe, and Even More So the Propaganda of Sending a Plenipotentiary Ambassador to Recognize the Puppet Organization Before the League of Nations Meeting, Sent a Telegraph to the League of Nations Investigation Team Yesterday to Uphold Justice. The Original Telegram Is As Follows: (To Gu Weijun, Representative in Beiping, Please Forward to Sir Lytton and All Members of the League of Nations Investigation Team. Japan Disregards Public Reason and Justice, Disregards International Covenants, Destroys the Nine-Power Treaty and the Pact of Paris, and Groundlessly Seizes Our Three Northeastern Provinces for Nearly a Year. Our Chinese Nation Loves Peace and Has Repeatedly Appealed to the League of Nations, Waiting Quietly for a Fair Disposition. However, Japan Has Become Even More Aggressive. While Your Team Is Conducting Investigations, It Dares to Display Force in Shanghai and Threaten Shanhaiguan, Intrude into Rehe, Seize Customs Posts, and, Using the Old Trick of Annexing Korea, Organize a Puppet Government. Recently, It Even Sent a Plenipotentiary Ambassador to Recognize the Puppet Organization. Its Disregard for the League of Nations Covenant, Destruction of the Nine-Power Treaty and the Pact of Paris Are Obvious Facts and Have Long Been Seen Through by All of You. We Hope You Will Uphold Justice, Report to the League of Nations As Soon As Possible, and Impose Powerful Sanctions. This Is Not Only the Fortune of Our Chinese Nation but Also the Fortune of the World's Future. Respectfully, the Educational Associations of All Districts of Shanghai. ) There Is Also a Telegram to the League of Nations, Which Is Largely the Same and Omitted.

Good News from the Mongolian Border Cavalry Regiment 113

Killed the Puppet Commander Wang Dianzhong

The Representative of the Mongolian Border Cavalry Commander in Shanghai Received a Telegram from Beiping Yesterday Stating, "Beiping Relayed a Telegram from Shenyang on the 6th. Liu Hexuan, Commander of the 9th Regiment of the Mongolian Border Cavalry Commander Cheng Changkui's Unit, Led His Troops in Fierce Battles with the Puppet State's Garrison Team in the Tianzhuangtai Area of Yingkou on a Recent Date. They Killed the Puppet Commander Wang Dianzhong and Captured Two Mortars, Two Mountain Guns, Four Machine Guns, and Seventy Rifles." It Is Verified That Wang Was a Former Subordinate of Zhang Zongchang. After the September 18th Incident, He Recruited Bandits in Dalian and Was Reorganized by the Japanese, Serving As the Commander of the 1st Brigade of the Provisional Army of Fengtian and Concurrent Commander for Bandit Suppression and Garrison in Seven Counties.

Various Organizations Held a Memorial Service for Ye Huijun Yesterday 114

Wang Xiaolai Said:

Mr. Ye Encouraged Us to Be "Foolishly Great" to the End

He Wishes Everyone to Rise Up and Continue Being "Foolishly Great"

Six Organizations, Including the Jiangsu Ninghu Municipal and County Rice Industry Association, the Shanghai Soybean and Rice Industry Association, the Miscellaneous Grains, Oil Cakes Industry Association, the Rice Milling Industry Association, the Rice Shop Industry Association, and the Miscellaneous Grains, Oil Cakes Exchange, Held a Memorial Service for Mr. Ye Huijun at the Miscellaneous Grains Association at No. 377 Minquan Road Yesterday Afternoon. The Entire Soybean, Rice, and Miscellaneous Grains Industry in the City Was Closed for One Day to Express Mourning.

Attendees: The People Who Participated in the Memorial Service Yesterday Included Mayor Wu Tiecheng (Represented by Luo Jingyou), Chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Wang Xiaolai, Standing Committee Member of the Municipal Party Pan Gongzhan, Businessmen Yu Qiaqing, Wang Yansong, Yu Zuoting, Lu Fengzhu, Lu Wenshao, Wu Zhihao, Ye Jiaxing, Qu Yingguang, Luo Qinghua, Fang Jiaobo, Xu Kesheng, Bankers Bei Songsun, Qian Xinzhi, Lin Kanghou, Official of the Public Concession He Dekui, Tax-Paying Chinese Association Xu Jilong, Yan Esheng, Commander of the Zhabei Defense Corps Wang Binyan, and Du Yuesheng, Wang Yiting. Organizations Present Included Representatives from the Shanghai Citizens' Promoting National Products Association, the National Products Maintenance Association, the Shanghai Miscellaneous Grains Association, the Rice Industry Association, Etc. The Boy Scouts of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Defense Corps Maintained Order.

Memorial Situation: At 2:30 PM, the Meeting Was Called to Order by Ringing a Bell.

The Public Security Bureau Music Team Played Funeral Music. After Performing the Rituals, Chairman Gu Xinyi Reported the Purpose of the Meeting and the Preparations, As Well As Mr. Ye's Biography. Next Was the Floral Offering, Followed by the Public Sacrifice by All Executive and Supervisory Committee Members of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce. Chairman Wang Xiaolai and Yan Esheng Read the Memorial Text. Next, the Management Committee of the Defense Corps, the Wuxi Rice Industry Organization, the Shareholders Association of the Miscellaneous Grains Exchange, the Broker Association, the Spiritualist Association, the Pudong Association, and the Six Organizations That Initiated the Memorial Service, Such As Soybean, Rice, and Miscellaneous Grains, Offered Sacrifices in Turn and Read the Memorial Text. Next Were Speeches from Various Circles, Ending with the Family Expressing Gratitude and Dispersing.

Mr. Ye's Biography: Mr. Ye's Given Name Was Zengming, Style Name Huijun, Also Known As Longsha Lazy Farmer. His Family Was From Shanghai and Resided in Gaohang Township on the Left Bank of the Huangpu River. His Family Had Been Engaged in Farming and Studying for Generations. His Respected Father, Zi Sui, Was a Shopkeeper and Died Early. At the Age of Fourteen, His Mother Sent Him to Shanghai to Study the Soybean and Rice Business. He Was Careful and Meticulous in His Work. After Graduating, He Was Entrusted with Important Responsibilities, and His Reputation Grew Daily. In His Spare Time, He Often Studied Poetry and Books and Had Many Literary Friends From All Over the Country. During the Sino-Japanese War of Jiawu, Our Teachers Were Defeated Repeatedly. He Grieved and Was Filled With Indignation, and He Had Reformist Ideas. During the Boxer Rebellion of Gengzi, National Affairs Were Almost Beyond Salvage. At This Point, He Knew That the Qing Society Was About to Collapse, So He Anxiously Worked With Like-Minded Local People to Seek Self-Strengthening. From Then On, He Presided Over the Shanghai Gymnastics Association and Then the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Regiment. He Was Very Active in His Duties and Worked Hard on Opium Prohibition. In the Late Qing Dynasty, He Joined the Tongmenghui and Secretly Planned Revolutionary Strategies With Shen Manyun, Zhu Shaoqi, and Other Comrades. He Organized the Patriotic Association and the National Chamber of Commerce Regiment, and He Was Elected As Their Leader. During the Wuchang Uprising, He, Chen Qimei, Li Pingshu, and Other Gentlemen Planned to Respond. On September 13 of That Year, He Supervised and Led the Regiment to Attack the Manufacturing Bureau, Fighting Fiercely for a Day and Night, and Capturing It. Shanghai Was Liberated, and the Overall Situation Was Settled. He Contributed Greatly. After the Establishment of the Shanghai Military Government, He Was Recommended As the Military and Political Commander, Presiding Over Local Defense, and Concurrent Chief of Staff of the Governor's Office. On New Year's Day of the Republic of China, He Led 300 Warriors to Accompany Mr. Sun Yat-Sen to the Capital to Assume the Position of Provisional President. He Was Appointed As the Police Chief of the Presidential Palace. Because His Duties in Shanghai Were Numerous and Burdensome, He Resigned. He Then Served As the Chief of the Tongfu Office's Railway Section. For Two Years, He Devoted Himself to Local Construction and Served As the Director of the Materials Department of the Shanghai Manufacturing Bureau. At That Time, President Yuan Shikai Conspired to Become Emperor. The Kuomintang's Punishment Failed. Because of His Previous Party Membership, Yuan Ordered Zheng Ruicheng, the Shanghai Garrison Commander, to Arrest Him, Offering 5,000 Gold Pieces. He Then Went to Japan in the East to Avoid Calamity Temporarily and Investigate the Politics of That Country. Later, He Lived in Dalian, Keeping a Low Profile. After Yuan's Defeat and Death, He Returned to Shanghai to Revitalize Industry. He Served As a Business Hub, Benefiting All Industries. He Was Particularly Involved in the Soybean, Rice, Miscellaneous Grains, and Oil Cakes Industries, Which Were Essential to People's Livelihoods. In Addition, He Participated in All Local Public Welfare Undertakings. Last Year, When the Sino-Japanese War Broke Out Again, He Grieved Greatly Over Liaoning and Songhu. He Devoted Himself to the Shanghai National Salvation Volunteer Army, Serving As a Backing for the National Army. However, the Authorities Advocated Peace, and His Righteous Indignation Could Not Be Vented. From Then On, His Body Often Felt Uncomfortable. He Accidentally Took a Laxative, Which Greatly Damaged His Vitality, and the Tumor in His Abdomen Was Hidden. This Spring, the Government Convened a National Crisis Conference in Luoyang. He Responded to the Call While Supporting His Sick Body. When the Boat Arrived in Nanjing, He Had to Turn Back Due to Physical Exhaustion. The Tumor in His Abdomen Became Severe, and All Medicines Failed. He Was Bedridden for Months and Died at the Age of Seventy on July 15 of the 21st Year of the Republic of China. When All Sectors Heard the News, They Were All Saddened Because of His Contributions to His Hometown and Country. The Shanghai Soybean, Rice, and Miscellaneous Grains Industries Were Even More Saddened Because They Had Benefited So Much From Him in the Past. They Gathered Together to Discuss and Schedule a Memorial Service to Express Their Mourning and Respect.

Mr. Ye's Will: A Special Issue Was Distributed at the Meeting, Carrying One of Mr. Ye's Calligraphic Works. From This, We Can See Mr. Ye's Lofty Spirit of Devoting Himself to the Revolution and Not Taking Credit for His Success. The Letter Reads, "Brother Remembers Since Separating From Jingmo in Shanghai in the Year of Xinhai, I Have Been Grateful for Your Attention, Despite My Mediocrity. I Heard From Friends Coming From the North That You and Gong Chang Often Ask About My Situation. I Can See Your Deep Friendship and High Regard, Which Is Endlessly Engraved in My Heart. However, Brother's Nature Is Foolish and Awkward, Out of Sync With the Times. When Yuan Was in Power, I Ran Around in Foreign Lands and Buried Myself in Penghu Island for Two Years. There Were Countless Setbacks. Recalling the Beginning of the Restoration, Colleagues All Know My Deeds. However, Thinking That I Am a Citizen, I Should Do My Best to Fulfill My Duties. How Can I Dare to Claim Credit? You Know Me, I Think You Have Long Seen Through It. Fortunately, the Republic Has Been Restored. Brother Returned to Shanghai From Dalian Last Winter. Old Friends Like Yingshi and Manyun Have Passed Away One After Another..." (Omitted Below) Summary of Speeches: Wang Xiaolai Said, "Mr. Ye Often Encouraged Us to Be 'Foolishly Great' to the End. Now, When Foreign Troubles and Domestic Woes Invade Each Other, Mr. Ye Has Passed Away. We Can Only Continue Mr. Ye's Spirit, Rise Up and Be 'Foolishly Great', and Fight Forward. Otherwise, It Will Be a Dead End." Pan Gongzhan Said, "Mr. Ye Has Three Spirits That Are Most Worth Remembering. First, He Is Diligent, Punctual, and Has a Strict and Uncompromising Spirit. Second, He Can Encourage the Younger Generation to Move Forward, With the Spirit of Helping Others Succeed and Helping Others Achieve." Third, He Is Always Optimistic, Does More and Says Less, and Has a Down-to-Earth Spirit. Wang Yansong Said, "On the One Hand, We Should Strive to Be a Backing for the Government and Seek to Improve the Status of the Country. On the Other Hand, We Hope That Business Organizations Will Consolidate to Improve Welfare and Relieve Suffering." Lin Kanghou Said, "Mr. Ye Has Three Characteristics: (1) Integrity, (2) Law-Abiding, and (3) Responsibility. It Is Truly Rare and Valuable." Qu Shao-yi Said, "Mr. Ye Is an Old Revolutionary But Has No Revolutionary Face. He Is Always Sincere and His True Nature Is Touching, Which Is Inimitable." Wang Shou-yi Said, "If Everyone Can Uphold Mr. Ye's Spirit of Serving the Country and Society, They Will Not Let Down Mr. Ye." Lu Wenshao Reported Mr. Ye's Contributions to the Soybean, Rice, and Miscellaneous Grains Industries, As Well As His Diligence and Fairness.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Announces That All Sectors Should Report Traitorous Merchants 115

Pay Attention to Their Transactions With Money Houses

And Where the Goods Are Sold

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce Announced to All Compatriots Yesterday, "To All Patriotic People in the City, Since Traitorous Merchants Violated the Covenant and Sold Japanese Goods on a Large Scale, We Have Been Assisted in Investigations by Enthusiastic People From All Walks of Life. We Are Sincerely Grateful for Any Information Received. However, This Kind of Treacherous Action Is Extremely Changeable and Bizarre. It Is Difficult to Obtain the Truth Through External Investigation. We Especially Hope That Employees and Shop Assistants Employed by Traitorous Merchants Will Uphold Their Patriotic Conscience and Notify This Association at Any Time by Letter. In Addition to Describing the Facts of Selling Japanese Goods in the Letter, the Two Most Important Points Are: (1) What Is the Brand Name of the Money House That the Traitorous Merchant Transacts With? (2) Where Are the Goods Sold? Please Do Not Avoid Suspicions and Resentments and Accurately Report to Help This Association, Which Is to Love and Protect the Country. This Is Most Desirable. Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Writes to the Coal Industry to Discuss National Coal Price Equalization Methods 116

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce Wrote to the Coal Industry Association Yesterday, "Respectfully, On the 10th of This Month, We Received a Letter From the Shipping Industry Association Stating That Coal for Ships Is a Major Expense, and Japanese Coal Is a Huge Amount of Sales in the Market. Since the National Crisis, Changing to National Coal Is the Desire of Everyone. However, the Current Price of Japanese Coal Is Only Six or Seven Taels per Ton, While National Coal Requires About Ten Taels per Ton, a Great Difference. Although Coal Consumption Varies From Ship to Ship, It Is Estimated That Each Ship Requires About 20 Tons per Day. If the Price Difference Is Three or Four Taels, Each Ship Will Need to Spend More Than a Hundred Taels per Month. This Means That Our Commercial Ships Pay the Difference Between the Value of National Coal and Japanese Coal, Which Requires Millions of Taels a Year. However, Foreign Ships Mostly Purchase Japanese Coal and Have Long-Term Contracts With Japanese Coal Merchants, Reducing Costs. Competing With Our Commercial Ships, Which Have Higher Coal Prices, Will Inevitably Lead to Losses, Which Will Lead to Stagnation. If Closed Down, Although National Coal Has Been Changed to, Shipping Rights Will Be Completely Occupied. This Is Not a Good Plan. No Wonder Shipowners Are Hesitant. In Order to Protect Shipping Rights and Promote National Coal, How Should We Negotiate the Difference in Prices of National Coal With the Coal Industry? We Urge the Government to Grant Special Relief to Protect National Rights and Maintain Commercial Shipping. For This Reason, We Have Written Truthfully. We Hope You Will Conduct Detailed Assessments and Implement Practical Methods to Address the Shared Interests of Shipping Rights and National Coal. We Have Recorded the Case and Sent a Letter. We Hope Your Association Will Formulate a Plan and Respond to the Meeting for Handling."

Yu Hongjun Discusses Recent Municipal Conditions 118

Financial Situation of This City in the 21st Year

Land Tax Proposed to Be Levied in the Recovered War Zone

Resolution to Protest Against Japanese Military Demonstration Across Borders; According to Central News Agency, Secretary-General Yu Hongjun of the Municipal Government Spoke to a Reporter From Central News Agency About Various Recent Situations in This City's District. The Financial Situation This Year: The Budget of This City for This Year Is About to Be Completed. The Situation Is That Expenditures Are Large and Income Is Small. The Income and Expenditure Offset, Short About Three Million Yuan. As a Remedy, the Municipal Government Decided to Take a Source-Opening Method. The Planned Expenditures for This Year Have Reached the Most Economical Limit. As for the Source-Opening Method, No Concrete Method Has Been Determined.

The Municipal Assembly Will Be Established: The Candidates for Shanghai Municipal Temporary Assembly Councilors Have Been Selected and Announced. Formal Letters of Appointment Can Be Officially Issued in Two or Three Days. All Matters That Should Be Carried Out Have Been Largely Arranged. It Is Expected That It Can Be Officially Established at the Beginning of Next Month.

Preparing to Levy Land Tax: The Shanghai War Zone Restoration Committee, in Order to Restore the Market in the Recovered War Zone, Suggested Levying a Land Tax. The Land Tax Is Different From the Field Tax. The Amount of Taxation Depends on the Price of the Land. Therefore, the Municipal Government Is Still Studying the Matter Carefully.

Japanese Military Demonstration Across Borders: Regarding the Matter of Japanese Troops in Shanghai Intruding Into Zhabei and Other Places for Demonstration, the Municipal Government Has Begun Investigating the Date and Time. The Municipal Government Will Certainly Protest Against This Kind of Out-of-Bounds Action.
