China Development Bank Inspection Report 122

The China Development Bank's first report on the issuance reserve examination stated that as of July 31st, 1932, the total amount of exchange notes issued by the bank's Shanghai, Ningbo, and Tianjin branches totaled 4,475,000 silver dollars.

Page 14

The total amount of the exchange note reserve was 4,475,000 silver dollars, including: (1) Cash reserve: 3,049,165.78 silver dollars, accounting for over 68% of the total reserve. This cash was stored in the Fuyuan Bank vault in the Shanghai area for 500,000 dollars, the Fukang Bank vault for 500,000 dollars, the Mercantile Bank vault for 500,000 dollars, the Hongkong and Shanghai Banking Corporation vault for 300,000 dollars, and the Shanghai, Ningbo, and Tianjin issuing vaults for 985,500 dollars. The remaining 263,665.78 dollars were deposited in Citibank, Mercantile Bank, Hongkong and Shanghai Banking Corporation, the Shanghai Municipal Council, and Shanghai Bank, etc. All branches and out-of-town exchange locations had official receipts. (2) Interbank deposit reserve: 452,222.22 silver dollars, accounting for over 10% of the total reserve. This reserve was deposited in 26 banks and financial institutions in the Shanghai area, including the Tianjin Bank of Communications, etc., all with official receipts. (3) Guarantee reserve: 973,612 silver dollars, accounting for slightly less than 22% of the total reserve. This reserve included various securities with a face value of 2,731,000 dollars guaranteed by customs duties, and public treasury certificates of the Shanghai Banking Association Joint Reserve amounting to 160,000 taels converted as above. The examination results showed that cash reserves and interbank deposit reserves accounted for more than 78% of the total reserve, while guarantee reserves accounted for slightly less than 22% of the total reserve. This report is submitted. August 13th, 1932, Accountant Wang Zikang, Board of Directors representatives Xu Jilun, Xu Busun, General Manager Qin Runqing, Head Office Manager Wang Boyuan.

British Merchant Public Bus Company Implements Hiring New Workers 123

After the strike of the British Merchant China Public Bus workers in the Public Concession, the company still tried to maintain traffic yesterday. The workers originally planned to demonstrate to the company yesterday morning but postponed it due to rain. Meanwhile, they expanded the organization of the strike committee and issued a notice to the workers. The company implemented hiring new workers today, and the situation is still serious. The details are recorded as follows:

Strict Precautions: The Sixth District Police Station of the Public Security Bureau and the Gordon Road Police Station of the Public Concession dispatched a large number of armed detectives to be stationed near the company on Connaught Road to prevent demonstrations by striking public bus workers. The strike committee, due to the heavy rain yesterday morning, ordered all workers to postpone the demonstration and instead convened a general meeting at the Renhe Tea House. More than 170 workers attended, and the following resolutions were made: (1) Due to the rain, four representatives were sent to negotiate with the company. (2) If the negotiation failed, it was decided that all members would participate in the armed picket line on the 14th to forcibly stop the buses and expel the White Russians. (3) They would not give up until their goals were achieved.

Protecting Traffic: The company yesterday tried to replace ticketing with inspection and fare checking, and managed to maintain operations. There were fourteen buses on Route 1, seven on Route 2, seven on Route 5, twenty-four on Route 9, and special military express buses. The Public Concession Police notified Chinese and Western detectives to provide strict protection along the way. Fortunately, no conflicts occurred in the evening. Yesterday morning, more than 40 unemployed Chinese workers suddenly came to the company's entrance on Connaught Road, claiming to be unemployed Chinese workers and requesting the company to give them jobs. Factory Director and General Manager of Vehicle Affairs Xiao Date ordered Indian police to expel them, and they dispersed immediately.

Expanding the Strike Committee: The strike committee officially announced to reporters from Xin Sheng News Agency yesterday that the company had previously designated six workers to form a delegation to discuss increasing wages in order to ease the atmosphere among the workers. The current strike committee has twelve members, including the six representatives designated by the company. They resigned after the strike was launched. A motion was made to dismiss them during the general meeting today, and it was decided to add five more members to the strike committee. They also insisted on opposing all scabs and traitors disrupting the strike. Regarding the Municipal Party Headquarters sending personnel to mediate, they opposed any mediation because this strike was a direct issue between workers and capitalists, and they believed that only by using the power of the masses could they win victory.

Hiring New Workers: The British Merchant China Public Bus Company adopted a tough policy towards the striking workers and announced that the strikers would be dismissed and new workers would be hired. Yesterday, Factory Director Xiao Date had already hired a batch of Chinese workers. It was decided that they would gather on the Bund of Nanjing Road this morning, and the company would dispatch a reserved bus to transport them to the company on Connaught Road for training. It was planned to restore public bus services on all routes in the shortest possible time. The company had also negotiated with the Public Concession Police in advance to have the police increase the number of armed detectives to protect the bus and maintain strict vigilance on the Bund of Nanjing Road to prevent striking workers from stopping it.

Party and Government Attitude: The Municipal Party Headquarters did send personnel to investigate the truth about the strike of ticket sellers of the British Merchant China Public Bus Company in the Public Concession to understand the truth, but the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau did not send personnel to investigate. It was rumored that a certain gentleman from the bureau was sent to Renhe Tea House yesterday and Zhu was sent to investigate together with the Municipal Party Headquarters the day before yesterday, but these were not true. The bureau had not made any statement regarding this strike as of yesterday.

Company Statement: The British Merchant Public Bus Company announced yesterday that the total number of striking workers after the sudden strike of ticket sellers was 301 ticket sellers and 48 Korean ticket inspectors. Chinese workers such as drivers, coppersmiths, sweepers, and ticket inspectors were not affected. As for the striking workers, they have not formally presented any conditions to the company. The company has now resolved through a board meeting to announce the dismissal of the strikers.

Social Affairs Bureau Formulates Principles for the Sanyou Industrial Company Factory Closure Case 124

Yesterday, a meeting was convened to solicit opinions. A formal mediation meeting is scheduled. The Social Affairs Bureau convened a meeting with labor and management yesterday to discuss the dispute over the closure of the Sanyou Industrial Company's Yinxiang Port factory, and proposed two principles for soliciting opinions. A formal meeting of the Labor-Management Mediation Committee is scheduled for mediation.

Two Principles: At 9:00 AM yesterday, the Social Affairs Bureau convened a meeting with labor and management. The attendees included Shen Jiucheng and Wang Xianhua, representatives of Sanyou Industrial Company; Gong Yuting and Xia Zhongzhao, representatives of the 7th District Cotton Textile Industry Union; Wu Guicheng, Chang Shaowen, Wu Qianyi, Zhang Tingliang, Liu Chunquan, Wang Chuncheng, Zhu Hongmo, Hong Jiaben, Wu Renfu, Yuan Zhixian, Xu Rongchang, Gu Shaozhen, Yang Changju, Chang Jiwen, Zhou Bingnian, Hu Xuechuan, Qu Fengzhi, Yao Tingshan, Hong Meishuo, Ma Youqing, Xu Chaonian, Tang Zhixiang, Wang Shaowen, Leng Shimo, Zhu Yushan, Wu Buyun, Zhu Dazhe, Huang Renlin, Bao Boyi, etc.; and Zhou Lianze from the Municipal Party Headquarters. Wang Xianqing, Director of the Mediation Section of the Social Affairs Bureau, presided over the meeting, and Wang Zhiqin recorded the minutes. The chairman first explained the purpose of the meeting, which was to enable labor and management to understand each other in order to reach an appropriate solution. He also stated that the Social Affairs Bureau had been actively mediating this case with the Municipal Party Headquarters, and two principles had been formulated: (1) to restore a portion of the work first; (2) to restore the rest when the opportunity arises. He specifically sought the opinions of both parties.

Labor and Management Opinions: Subsequently, Shen Jiucheng, the representative of the management, stated the difficulties of not being able to open the factory and expressed that the company's pain over the closure was greater than that of the unemployed. He also submitted a written statement from the company, detailing the various reasons why it could not resume work, stating that the company had exhausted all efforts and considered it carefully. The following is a summary of the statement: (1) The proposal to partially resume work: Given the company's dire situation, there is no hope. Partial resumption of work is also considered difficult. (2) The proposal to relocate to the Hangzhou factory: The Hangzhou factory itself is a yarn factory, although it has weaving machines, it is also for women's work. Recently, due to the sluggish market, most of the original female workers have also suffered unemployment. Therefore, relocation to Hangzhou is absolutely impossible in fact. (3) The proposal to temporarily suspend work at the Yinxiang factory and reopen when the opportunity arises: The Yinxiang factory has been severely ravaged and destroyed, and it has suffered deep wounds and there is no hope of recovery. Therefore, it is impossible to reopen in fact. The labor representative, Yu Ting, explained the various sufferings of the workers since the closure, as well as the company's operating conditions over the years. The workers must resume work now, or at least resume a portion of the work. Subsequently, representatives from both parties expressed their opinions, and as a result, because the opinions of both parties failed to converge, it was decided to end the negotiations. Scheduled Mediation: At the end, the chairman stated that the Social Affairs Bureau would formally convene mediation in the shortest possible time. If mediation fails to be established by the deadline, it can only be submitted to the Municipal Government for arbitration according to law. It is hoped that both parties will give it serious consideration. At the same time, the management representative also stated: (1) The company has already considered it carefully and cannot think of any way. It is hoped that it will not be delayed any longer and that arbitration will be carried out according to law immediately. (2) The meal allowance was originally a temporary relief, but it has been borne for a long time and cannot be continued.

Pudong Native Association Donates to the Northeast Volunteer Army and Refugees 126

Advance remittance of 5,000 yuan

Shanghai Arsenal Has Been Closed 128

Jinling Factory Director Li Ganqing Returned to Beijing Yesterday: The merger of the Jinling and Shanghai arsenals has been handled by the Shanghai Arsenal Committee. The Jinling Arsenal recently sent Factory Director Li Ganqing to Shanghai to contact Shanghai Factory Director Song Shijun to negotiate the merger. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Continues to Receive Reports on the Case of Selling Japanese Rice 129

In addition to the YUKang warehouse Japanese rice of TongXingtai

There are also 100,000 bags in Yangjiadu, Pudong. Regarding the case of Shu Zhanyuan selling Japanese rice, after the exposure by the Smuggler Investigation Team, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce requested a thorough investigation, and it was found that the red-marked Japanese rice deposited in the YUKang warehouse, in addition to those that have already been shipped out, there are still more than 9,100 bags, which are all owned by TongXingtai Rice Firm. The list was immediately reported to the Standing Committee, and the Standing Committee decided to appoint two Supervisory Committee members to jointly form a special review committee with representatives from the grain and soybean rice industry. The investigation team was also notified to submit evidence to the association before the 15th for review. Now the Chamber of Commerce has received the third report from the team. In addition to the Japanese rice stored in YU Kang by TongXingtai, there is also a huge amount of rice stored in the warehouses in Pudong and Yangjiadu. The current owner, He Jiachun, has secretly left Shanghai for Nagasaki because the matter has been exposed. The original letter is recorded as follows: "Dear Sirs of the General Chamber of Commerce, I would like to inform you that the rice merchant He Jiachun is the owner of TongXingtai Rice Firm. His methods of selling inferior rice are no different from those of the merchant Shu Zhanyuan, and they can be called brothers in arms. Our team has briefly stated this in the letter exposing Shu Zhanyuan, and now after further investigation, this merchant He Jiachun is from the Japanese merchant Nozawa Assistant Foreign Firm and has always colluded with the Japanese, which is well known. The Public Association of Grain, Oil, and Cake inspected He Jiachun's stored rice and found that there were three batches of inferior rice, which were very suspicious, and the punishment method has not yet been determined. Now your association has investigated the YUKang warehouse and found that the more than 9,000 bags of inferior rice of TongXingtai are all owned by He Jiachun. Our team has learned that this merchant He Jiachun has many tricks. In addition to hoarding a large amount of inferior rice in YUKang, he also has 100,000 bags of inferior rice stored in Pudong and Yangjiadu. We earnestly request that your association urgently punish him, notify the warehouses to stop shipping the goods, and that He Jiachun, knowing that the evidence is conclusive and the circumstances are serious, knows that it is difficult to avoid severe punishment, and is trying to clear out the rice stored in Pudong overnight and secretly leave Shanghai to Nagasaki temporarily. It is impossible to allow such a villainous merchant to be at large. How should your association punish him severely? It should be handled immediately. At this critical moment, it is urgent to act quickly. Our team believes that all the inferior rice stored in YUKang and Pudong by the merchant should be confiscated and used as supplies for the Northeast Volunteer Army. As for He Jiachun himself, in addition to the punishment of parading him in a wooden cage, his personality should be declared bankrupt, so that one can be warned to prevent future merchants from daring to do so. This is an opportunity to improve the future of trade. I hope your association will take action quickly. In addition, the merchant Shu Zhanyuan is still trying to defend himself in the newspapers, which is very annoying. Our team does not need to repeat it and has collected and sorted out all the evidence to compile a written report, which will be sent to your association's special committee for handling as soon as possible. Correspondingly, we are writing to inform you. We wish you all the best, from the Merchant Investigation Team."

Jardine Matheson's Telephone Line Cut Off 130

Taxpayer Association Sends Letter to the Municipal Council to Strive for Rights

The Taxpayer Association previously sent a letter to the Municipal Council regarding the exemption of telephone charges in areas affected by the war, and has now received a reply from the Council stating that the Waterworks Company and the Telephone Company have indicated that they can handle the matter. The method is roughly the same as the exemption of general tax. The relevant letters are recorded as follows:

Taxpayer Association's Letter to the Municipal Council: "According to the letter from Jardine Matheson, the company's business at 1459 Wusong Road was located in the most dangerous area during the January 28th Incident, and the employees fled, and all telephone number 41093 was also immediately discontinued. On May 8th, the Shanghai Telephone Company sent a letter urging to pay the telephone bill of 39 taels of silver from February to the end of July. Our company sent a letter requesting a quarter of exemption, but received no reply. On July 3rd, the company sent another letter demanding two quarters of arrears and threatened to cut the line. On July 4th, our company sent another registered letter stating the previous letter requesting a quarter of exemption and stated that this type of case had been handed over to the Chinese Taxpayer Association for negotiation. Before the resolution, please reserve the right to use it. The company did not reply and cut off the telephone line on August 4th. On August 5th, our company sent someone to negotiate, and Fei Erpei, from the accounting department of the company, knew that he was in the wrong and agreed to waive the reconnection fee to reconnect the line. He still ignored the exemption. However, although our company was only cut off the line for one day, the losses were huge. During the war, as our company was located in this location, the business was suspended, which is known to the whole city. Since the telephone was not used, there is naturally no obligation to pay the fee. The company's arbitrary oppression is disregarding public reason. I don't know what extent your association has negotiated for this type of case. I have long admired your association as the mouthpiece of the concession, and I hope you will uphold justice." The letter also included a copy of the company's letter to the Shanghai Telephone Company. "It is noted that the telephone fee was free during the war, as explained by your council's letter No. 140 on June 17th, which has been handled by the company separately. Now that our association has received such a report, the so-called (uniform and consistent) (no deception to children and adults) method, the telephone company does not want to adopt it at all, and for not paying the phone bill due to reasons beyond the control of the party, it uses high-pressure means to cut off the line. Although the party has argued with reason and regained its original state, the company's act of infringement and the fact that it exercises its rights to infringe on others cannot be eliminated, then the request that the company should bear civil liability for compensation cannot be said to be unreasonable. According to the previous letter, we should send a letter to your council to quickly correct the company's fault."

Taxpayer Association's Reply to Jardine Matheson: "In reply to your letter on August 8th, regarding the Shanghai Telephone Company's refusal to exempt wartime usage fees and the disconnection of the line, we have learned that the company is so overbearing and extremely high-handed. If your company had not argued with reason, the company would have obtained an unjust enrichment through its act of infringement. As for the free telephone during the war, our association has negotiated with the Public Concession Council, and according to the letter from the Council on May 23rd, No. 140, regarding the exemption of telephone and water fees during the war in Hongkou, the two companies have stated that if it is indeed necessary to exempt, they are willing to stop charging immediately. The method of stopping charging is roughly the same as the exemption of general tax, but because the regulations have not been finalized, we can only handle it separately for each user. Most of the users who sent letters to the two companies requesting exemption have been satisfactorily resolved. However, due to contractual relations, water and telephone in the areas affected by the war in Shanghai are still supplied as usual. If the so-called exemption method is implemented excessively, the burden will still fall on other users, which does not seem appropriate. We are writing to reply and hope you will protect yourself according to law. Our association will immediately send a letter to the Council requesting correction."

Preparations by All Sectors in Luodian Town to Commemorate Ji Hetsun 131

Luodian Town, Baoshan County, since the Shanghai Incident, the head of the local defense regiment, Ji Hetsun, personally led the team to defend the area and maintain local security, doubling his hard work. Later, when our army retreated to Baoshan, Regiment Leader Ji was arrested by the enemy forces. Without asking for any reason, he was shot to death, and his body was thrown into the Hamai. It was only recently discovered, and his whole body was rotten. Local people from all walks of life, in order to recognize the loyalty, bravery, and dedication of Martyr Ji, who sacrificed himself for the country, specially plan to hold a memorial service to comfort the loyal soul. Shi Jingbin, Qian Peisheng, Sun Danshi, Zhu Lenglin, and others were appointed to be responsible for the preparations, which are scheduled to be held on September 4th. All expenses will be automatically donated by all sectors.

Jishanhui Obtains Disaster Situation in Liu'an, Huoshan, Zhengyang, etc. 133

The China Jishanhui recently received a report from Wang Dusheng and Zhang Zepu, the directors of the refugee camps in Liu'an, Huoshan, and other counties in northern Anhui, stating that since the counties of northern Anhui, including Liu'an and Huoshan, were occupied by bandits, the people were displaced and many died. At a time of prolonged drought and rampant epidemics, people died not from bandits but from hunger; if not from hunger, then from disease. Dusheng and others witnessed the tragedy and could not bear to describe it. In addition, the number of deaths increased daily, medicines were in short supply, and coffins were depleted. The southern wind was steaming, and the stench filled the air. Everyone living here felt threatened. Dusheng and others repeatedly deliberated and decided to move the refugees from the Dawangmiao No. 2 Refugee Camp to a safe location. However, Bengbu has been repeatedly disturbed, and the official offices have been destroyed. It is impossible to find suitable houses. As a last resort, we can only write to your association, hoping that you will have mercy and add funds in order to rent a temporary house or build some thatched sheds so that we can relocate as soon as possible. As for the dead refugees, most are wrapped in straw mats. The dead are indeed tragic, but the health of the living is even more important. We plan to provide coffins to the dead refugees, according to the size of their families, and bury them deeply in wooden boxes. We respectfully ask for your decision and reply. The seasonal medicines mailed a few days ago have been received and distributed, but the epidemic is severe and too many medicines are needed. We hope you will generously donate more to save lives. In view of this situation, the association feels extremely sympathetic. In the midst of being unable to plan, we reluctantly save to provide some help, and have telegraphed a reply to consider renting a house to provide coffins and send more medicines in the hope of preserving the lives of the refugees in one case out of ten thousand.

Those Who Die of Epidemics Should Be Buried Immediately 135

County Government Issues Order to Advise

The Shanghai County Government, in view of the fact that after this year's war, the weather has been hot in summer and epidemics have been prevalent, with successive deaths of the people, in order to prevent the spread of epidemics and maintain public safety, yesterday issued an order to all public security bureaus that, for all people who die of epidemics in the territory, no storage should be allowed, and they should be buried within three days. Those who resist and disobey should be enforced. On the one hand, the district chiefs were ordered to instruct the township chiefs to advise burial.

The warship has not yet returned to China because the construction costs have not been fully paid. Therefore, the Ministry of the Navy is requesting funds from the National Government.

Because the company failed to register in accordance with the Company Law, China's First Sound Film Company published advertisements in major newspapers in this city to solicit shares. Because the registration procedures were not followed in accordance with the provisions of the Company Law and submitted to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for approval and registration, the Bureau was inevitably concerned with the potential for malpractice. Local News Two

A Little Kidnapping Victim Rescued from a Small Boat in Haig Road River 146

Three Kidnappers Arrested One Escaped After Throwing Away His Gun

At around 9:00 AM yesterday, Jin Jiulin, the superintendent of the Special Agency of the French Concession Police, received a tip that a kidnapping bandit named Han Youwen would be passing by Pingjili Road and requested the police to arrest him immediately. Superintendent Jin immediately ordered detectives Li Yaolong, Zhang Ziying, Qin Youyu, and Cai Jinzhang to disguise themselves and wait in ambush. Shortly after, Han came swaggering by and was intercepted at the entrance of the Pingan Hotel. Han confessed that there were two accomplices, Jiangbei natives Wang Shaoqing and Yu Dashunzi, hiding in a bungalow at 5 Taopeng Road. The detectives, accompanied by Han, and together with the Yulin Road Police, arrested Wang and Yu at the address and brought them directly to the French Concession Police Station. After questioning by the police chief, the two confessed that they had a seven-year-old kidnapping victim, the son of Qian Guanjin, a resident of 7 Pu'enluo Se Road, who was kidnapped from Qian's home on July 20th. The victim's name is Miaofu and he is currently hidden in a small boat in the river at the border of Haig Road and the French Concession. The detectives, after hearing the confession, at 3:00 PM, accompanied by the two bandits, took cars and rushed to the address. They also notified the police chief of the local Public Security Bureau and rushed to intercept a small boat, rescuing the victim on the spot. However, the bandit guarding the victim, who was watching from the shore, saw the police arrive and knew that things were not going well. He hastily threw a pistol into the river and escaped. The detectives chased after him, but were unable to catch him. They retrieved the pistol and, along with the victim, brought him to the police station. They notified the victim's family to take him home first. The bandits were separately detained pending a strict investigation in court.

Police Officer Disappears While Arresting Gamblers 147

Bound by Boatmen and Thrown into the Sea Water Patrol Accuses Boatmen of Murder

A group of boatmen were gambling on a Huangsha boat in Gaoqiao, Pudong the other day. When the water patrol officers went to arrest the gamblers, a boatman named Ye Hexin from Ningbo fell into the river and died. At that time, the family immediately filed a complaint with the court and the police station for investigation. Unexpectedly, one of the police officers was also missing. After investigation by the water patrol, it was found that when one of the police officers went on board the ship, he was bound by the boatmen and thrown into the sea. Therefore, the police accused the boatmen of murder and immediately sent police to arrest the boatmen Xing A'ao, Wu A'tu, Wu Quanlin, Wu Haolin, Wu Jinglin, etc., and presented them to the Public Security Bureau. Yesterday, they were transferred to the local court for interrogation.

Bold and Daring Unscrupulous Merchants Change Inferior Goods into National Goods 148

Changing Japanese Yarn into Double Whale Trademark

The Unscrupulous Merchant Cai Zisheng is handed over to the Public Security Bureau. Cai Zisheng, a native of Xiaoshi, Zhejiang, used to specialize in selling enemy goods. After the January 28th Incident, Cai did not dare to be blatant, but still operated privately. Recently, he has intensified his efforts and even changed the appearance of Japanese yarn, labeling it with the Double Whale trademark of the Qinfeng Yarn Factory, and openly transported it to other ports for sale. This was discovered by Zeng Yi, a customer of the Qinfeng Factory, who immediately began investigating. On the 10th of this month, it was discovered that Cai was storing the counterfeit enemy goods at the North Railway Station, intending to transport them to Xiaoshi. Zeng immediately reported to the Railway Police Department, which dispatched police to detain all 28 packages of enemy goods. Cai was strictly pursued. At 6:00 PM the other day, Zeng learned that Cai was hiding in Room 516 of the Central Hotel in the Public Concession. He reported to the Fifth District Public Security Bureau, which dispatched detective Xin Jingsheng and the old gate detective Qiu Sijiu to arrest Cai at the address and take him back to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, Ye Fu Kang, the lawyer hired by the Qinfeng Factory, arrived at the First Special Court Criminal Division I to act as an agent. He stated that the case was requested by the Public Security Bureau and that the police had sufficient evidence. Therefore, the lawyer did not object to the requested transfer. Subsequently, Zeng Yi submitted a petition stating that the yarn produced by the factory was coarse and black, while the counterfeit enemy goods of the defendant were fine and white, which was obvious proof. When questioned, the defendant denied passing off enemy goods as national goods. Lawyer Ye presented various evidence to prove this. Judge Feng Shide ruled that Cai Zisheng was allowed to be handed over to the Public Security Bureau's detectives for interrogation, as the case was extremely clear.

Exposure of Impersonating a Military Officer 149

Shen Luqin Claims to be a Whampoa Student Serving in the 13th Brigade of the 5th Division His Deception Was Exposed When He Intervened in a Dung Dumping Incident A Large Number of Envelopes, Stamps, and Cards Were Also Confiscated

Shen Luqin, a native of Shaoxing, 33 years old, resides with his father-in-law at 48 Anren Street because he is dissatisfied with the actions of his stepmother after his father's death. Shen usually claims to be a graduate of the 4th class of the Infantry Department of the Whampoa Military Academy and is currently a major staff officer in the headquarters of the 13th Brigade of the 5th Division of the Army. He has this rank printed on his business cards and always wears a military uniform, carries a belt, wears leather shoes, and leggings, appearing very energetic, like a senior military officer. Residents in the vicinity, seeing his behavior, all assumed that he must be in an important position in the military, so they did not argue with him whenever incidents occurred. A woman surnamed Zhang from Zhang Rongchang's carpentry shop at 52 Zhangjia Lane, Anping Street, Xinbei Gate, poured excrement from a chamber pot into a ditch the other day. Shen happened to see it and immediately stepped forward to intervene. The woman argued with him a little. Afterwards, Shen reported the situation to the Municipal Health Bureau, which sent a letter to the Municipal Public Security Bureau, which in turn ordered the Second Precinct of the First District to send police to investigate. After receiving the order, Bao Wuqiao, the director of the precinct, dispatched service personnel Fan Quanzhong to investigate. Seeing that Shen's business card stated that he was a graduate of the Whampoa Military Academy, and suspecting that he was a classmate, Fan went to visit Shen. After Shen received him, Fan noticed that his behavior was strange and immediately inquired about the various situations of the Whampoa Military Academy and the 5th Division. However, Shen's answers were fabricated. Fan questioned him again and again. Finally, Shen suddenly said, "Please don't say more. My brain is confused now. I don't know anything." At this point, Fan realized that he was impersonating a military officer and swindling and cheating. He immediately arrested him and searched his bedroom, discovering a seal of the Deputy Adjutant's Office of the 2nd Cavalry Brigade of the 5th Division of the National Revolutionary Army, dozens of envelopes printed with the words "Headquarters," many cards of Chen Lin, the Quartermaster Director of the 26th Regiment of the 13th Brigade of the 5th Division of the National Revolutionary Army, and various stamps, which were taken back to the precinct pending preliminary review.

Italian Ship Damaged En Route 150

Himalaya Ship Lost in the Suez Canal

Goods Arrive a Month Late Damaged En Route

The Himalaya, a cargo ship of the Italian Postal Ship Company, was on its ninth voyage from Italy to the Far East. The ship was carrying a large number of artificial silk, machinery, foreign paper, and hardware, more than 1,000 tons to Shanghai. Yesterday, the ship sent a telegram stating that it had been damaged in the Suez Canal. The ship's machinery was completely destroyed and it could no longer sail. The Italian country's ship was sent to rescue it.

Towed Back to the Country The Himalaya ship, with a deadweight of 7,000 tons, is a newly built motor ship of the company, specializing in Central Europe, carrying cargo and not taking passengers. Now, due to the impact of the hull, the damage is very large, and the machine room is even more serious. The ship has stopped coming to Shanghai and the company has sent a ship to tow it back to the country for major repairs. Originally scheduled to arrive on September 5, it has now been rescheduled.

Delayed Arrival of Goods The goods on board were purchased by Hakka merchants in Shanghai and were originally scheduled to arrive on September 5 for unloading and delivery. Now, the Italian Postal Company continued to telegraph that the goods on the Himalaya ship, which were not damaged, have been transferred to the Coltana ship and will arrive in Shanghai on October 6, about a month later than the original date. Yesterday, the local Italian Ship Company has notified the merchants.

After the Nitriding Fur Factory Was Destroyed, a Large Batch of Foreign Fur Was Suddenly Found Missing 156

The China Nitriding Fur Factory at 2-4 Zhaofuli, Baoshan Road, Zhabei, was abandoned by its personnel during the January 28th Shanghai War. After the ceasefire, the manager returned to the factory to inspect, but found that the buildings had been reduced to ashes and rubble, a huge loss of 40,000 to 50,000 yuan. They could only sigh in vain. Suddenly, on the 9th of this month, a young man with a generous appearance came to the Changtai Fur Shop at 225 Sichuan Road A, selling four boxes of foreign fur worth more than 700 yuan. He said that the goods were piled up in the Guangtailai Inn at 107 Aiduya Road. If anyone wanted to buy them, they could go to see them. The manager of the shop, Chen Shouzhi, went to see the samples and was very surprised because the goods were the stolen goods of the China Nitriding Fur Factory, as evidenced by the ADH three-letter code on the fur (Chen is also a shareholder of the China Nitriding Fur Factory). Chen immediately notified Jiang Baochu, the manager of the factory, to come to the scene to identify the goods, and then reported to the Dazimingzhong Patrol Room. Detectives Wang Rusong and Wang Maonan were dispatched to arrest Chen Yin, a Cantonese man who was harboring the stolen goods, and brought him to the patrol room. Yesterday, he was transferred to the Second Criminal Division of the Second Special Court. The lawyer of the patrol room, Yuan Jiaheng, stated the case, saying that the defendant had committed the crime of receiving stolen goods in Article 376 of the Criminal Law and requested that he be investigated according to law. Detective Wang Maonan said that he was ordered to investigate the other day and the owner of the inn stated that Chen Junda, a Cantonese man, came to Guangtailai Inn in April and rented Room 48. Four boxes of fur were transported from Wuxi, which was the stolen goods in the case and were piled up in the inn and could not be sold. Chen returned to Guangdong on May 17th and still owed the inn a large amount of room and board, stating that he would return to Shanghai soon and repay the debt after selling the goods. After Chen left, on July 13, Chen Yin, the defendant in the case, came to the inn with a letter from Chen Junda to Wang Jinbao, the manager of Guangtailai, saying that the goods were entrusted to Chen Yin to be sold in Shanghai, and Chen was also responsible for the outstanding room and board. As for where the goods came from, he did not know. The plaintiff Chen stated the situation of the theft. Chen Yin confessed that the fur was actually entrusted by his relative Chen Junda in Guangdong to be sold in Shanghai and he did not know its origin. Judge Wu Fanglian verified the confession and ordered the defendant to be returned to custody and ordered Chen Junda to be brought to court for questioning within seven days.

Huang Biru Can't Bear the Harassment.

Defiling Someone First and Then Selling Them 163

Zhou Yinhua's Fate Is Unfortunate.

Evil Men Cannot Escape the Law. Zhou A'lai, from Ningbo, works as a butcher's helper at Tao Xianggen's pig butchery in Taojiazhai, Zhongshan Road, Zhabei. He has a daughter named Yinhua, who is now 14 years old. When Yinhua was five years old, her mother passed away, so A'lai entrusted Yinhua to his sister, Mrs. Chen, at 27 Siwen Lane, Datong Road, where she was raised until now, for nine years. Unexpectedly, Mrs. Chen also passed away last year. Mrs. Chen's daughter, Chen Fuying, 22 years old, was a worker at a silk factory. Since her mother's death, she has been unable to support herself, so she also recommended Yinhua to work at the silk factory. On the 5th of this month, Zhang Yongxing, the owner of the clock shop at 606 Xinzha Road, and Ke Heshang, a member of the Xinzha District Fire Brigade number 81, came to Chen Fuying's place, claiming that Yinhua was growing up and that it was time for her to marry. They said that Ke's colleague, Zhou Hongyuan, a firefighter number 206, was single and of good standing, and they had come to act as matchmakers for Yinhua. However, they needed to take her to meet him first, and if they were compatible, they would notify them for the formal betrothal. Chen Fuying, along with Zhang and Ke, first took Zhou Yinhua to a teahouse and then to Zhou Hongyuan's house at 123 Guizhou Road. That evening, Zhou's cousin forcibly raped Yinhua. The next day, they colluded and sold Yinhua into a brothel in the French Concession for 300 yuan. Meanwhile, Zhang Yongxing, Ke Heshang, and Chen Fuying met with Zhou A'lai in Zhabei a few days ago, saying that they had arranged a marriage for Yinhua and received a bride price of 150 yuan. When Zhou asked where she had been betrothed, they refused to reveal it. The day before yesterday, Zhou A'lai, along with Tao Xianggen and others, went to Xinzha Road to argue with Zhang Yongxing, resulting in a quarrel. The police saw this and brought Zhang and others to the Xinzha Police Station. Under questioning, Zhang confessed to the previous events. Detective Cui Chengke was then dispatched to arrest Zhou Hongyuan, Chen Fuying, and Ke Heshang successively and detained them separately with Zhang Yongxing. However, after being sold into the brothel, Zhou Yinhua refused to receive guests and was abused by the madam. She secretly escaped the day before yesterday and went to Zhabei to look for them but could not find them. Returning to Chen Fuying's house in Siwen Lane, she was spotted by the patrol police, who brought her to the police station. Yesterday morning, she was escorted to Criminal Division 2 of the First Special District Court. Police lawyer Wang Yaotang accused the four defendants of violating Article 25, Sections 1 and 2 of the Criminal Law, for obstructing family integrity. However, because the victim, Zhou Yinhua, was raped, she needed to be sent to the hospital for examination. Therefore, he requested that she be temporarily detained at the Jiliang Institute and that because accomplices were still at large, he requested an extension. Subsequently, Zhou A'lai, along with Tao Xianggen and Tan Xueqing, surrendered themselves, explaining the previous events. The victim, Zhou Yinhua, testified that she was raped by Zhou Hongyuan's cousin and sold into a brothel in the French Concession, forced to receive guests, and that she escaped due to the beatings. She also identified Zhou Hongyuan's cousin, who was also present in court, overhearing the proceedings. The Chinese and Western detectives then apprehended Zhou's cousin and took him back to the police station for investigation in order to prosecute him. The defendants then hired lawyers Fan Gang and others to defend them, requesting bail. Judge Wu Tingqi questioned each defendant individually, and their responses were mostly evasive. He then ordered each defendant to be detained separately and rescheduled the hearing for seven days later. Zhou Yinhua was temporarily sent to the Jiliang Institute for shelter.

More than 20 people attended, including Xue Wenyuan, Jiang Wenfang, Sheng Xinru, and Shen Xinjiu. Swindled When Exchanging Silver Dollars for Banknotes 165

For the Sake of Greed for Fifty Copper Coins.

Da Dexin Lost 45 Yuan. Yesterday afternoon, two young men in Western suits, with refined manners, suddenly arrived at Da Dexin Oil Shop on Muddy Beach Main Street in Pudong, holding fifty silver dollars wrapped in paper, and asked to exchange them for banknotes, willing to give one copper coin per dollar. The shop owner, thinking he could gain fifty copper coins, agreed. He opened the paper package, inspected the silver dollars, and found no counterfeits. After examining them, he placed them on the counter and took out the banknotes in the shop, but he only had forty yuan, which was not enough. Unexpectedly, the two young men suddenly claimed that the money was for paying wages and that if there were not enough banknotes, silver dimes could be substituted. The shop owner scrambled together silver dimes, but only managed to gather five yuan. Together with the banknotes, there were forty-five yuan, still five yuan short. He then took five silver dollars from the package brought by the two young men and went to the Yulong Money Exchange across the street to exchange them for banknotes. After finishing, he returned to the shop and handed over forty-five silver dollars and five silver dimes to the two young men. The two young men thanked him and left. The shop owner then recounted the silver package, only to find that upon opening the package, all forty-five of the snow-white silver dollars (because five yuan had already been exchanged at the money exchange across the street) had vanished. All that remained was an iron cylinder, about the size of a silver dollar and about five inches long. The cylinder was filled with lead, its weight approximately the same as fifty silver dollars. At this point, the shop owner realized he had been deceived. He rushed out to look for the two young men, but they had disappeared. The deceptive tactics in Shanghai are becoming increasingly strange. Businessmen must be extra vigilant.

Burglary on Yulin Road Last Night 166

Thieves Fired Shots as a Show of Force and Fled

An Apprentice Shot and Killed. At approximately 8:30 PM last night, while the Dachangxiang General Merchandise Store at 524 Yulin Road in Hongkou was preparing to close accounts, two burglars suddenly appeared, wearing blue and white short shirts and trousers. One burglar held a gun, guarding the entrance and monitoring the shop owner, forbidding him from making any noise. The other unarmed burglar entered the shop and attempted to rob the cash register. Jiang Zisheng, an apprentice at the store, happened to come out from the back and, seeing the situation, rushed forward to grab the cash register and shouted loudly. Seeing that things were not going well, the armed burglar fired a shot at the apprentice and fled. As he exited the door, he fired another shot into the air. Several off-duty police officers happened to be outside nearby, enjoying the cool air. They joined in the pursuit. Seeing this, the burglars fired another shot at the crowd and turned towards Yangzhou Road, escaping without a trace. The injured apprentice was shot in the right chest, a vital area. Due to excessive bleeding, he died before he could be treated. The Yulin Road Police Station sent a hearse to take the body to the mortuary for examination.

Letter Received

Dear Sir,

Having read in your esteemed newspaper's local news column an article about a Yanghzou woman, Pei Yin, accusing Ms. Xu et al. of abducting her son, I was extremely astonished. Upon investigation, no court hearing or interrogation has taken place yesterday, so where did the quoted statement come from? It is apparent that the submitter fabricated the facts with ulterior motives. The content is completely inconsistent with the truth. As this concerns reputation, please correct it immediately. Enclosed is a letter from the Nanhui County Relief Center, which reads: "Received your letter stating that Ms. Xu Jiping has informed us that she dismissed her maid, Pei Yin, who then insisted that her son, Pei Sanzi, was placed in your orphanage at Ms. Jiping's suggestion, through the introduction of Pan Keping. The lawyer's letter is absurd and intended for extortion. We previously entrusted your law firm to sternly refute it. Now, Pei Yin has fabricated facts and falsely accused Ms. Jiping et al. of abduction to the Shanghai Second Special District Court. We have received a summons and specifically entrust your law firm to legally prosecute Pei Yin for false accusation, etc." We request that your institution provide detailed information on Pei Sanzi's admission and current situation to clarify the truth. According to our records, Pei Sanzi was admitted on March 26th, 1931. At that time, a man claiming to be Yin Qishan brought an orphan to the center, claiming the child was his nephew, named Pei Sanzi, whose parents were deceased and no one was able to care for him. He stated that he was going out to seek work and could not afford to take the child with him, requesting that we take care of the orphan. The center, seeing his pitiful situation, immediately ordered the orphanage to admit and educate him. Later, in November 1931, the director of the orphanage reported that citizen Zhang Huating had submitted a request to take back the orphan Pei Sanzi to raise him as his heir. With a guarantee from a public security officer and after verification, we approved the release in accordance with Article 8 of the orphanage's regulations. Pei Sanzi currently resides at 25 Bai Guo Shu, Hanximen, Nanjing, at Zhang Huating's home. The above is the content of the letter. Please investigate and inform us accordingly. This is a reply to Lawyer Hu Jue, from Nanhui County Relief Center, July 20th, 1932." We hope you will publish this together to clarify the truth and clear up any confusion. To the Editor of Shenbao, from Lawyer Hu Jue, August 13th.

Free Talk

Two One Branch Talk

The Tongue is Flat 184

— Zhanlu

All women who can speak have a dictionary of colloquialisms in their bellies. They quote them very aptly. Praising is done with a colloquialism, and condemning is also done with a colloquialism. As long as one remembers many colloquialisms, one can be eloquent.

When praising an ugly person, one says: "An ugly woman has the face of a lady." But if one despises ugliness, one simply says: "Ugly people are always acting strange." To say that all Bodhisattvas are the same, one simply says: "A thousand Buddhas, ten thousand Buddhas, are all one Buddha." To say that all Bodhisattvas are not the same, one simply quotes another saying, called: "Each temple has its own Bodhisattva."

To encourage people from the lower classes, one quotes: "A hero is not afraid of a humble origin." If one

detests people from the lower classes, one should say: "Good insects don't come out of thatched nests." To ridicule those who are stingy, one always says: "Ill-gotten wealth is like soup poured on snow." If one wants to defend them, one should say: "Righteousness does not manage wealth," which shows that the rich don't really need righteousness. To say that a person shouldn't be too kind, one can say: "Kind people are easily bullied, and good horses are easily ridden." To say that a person can be kind, one can also

say: "People fear the wicked, but Heaven doesn't; people bully the kind, but Heaven doesn't."

Why are there such different interpretations when quoting the same colloquialism? I have an analogy: it's like the oars on a boat. On a winding waterway, the oars can be used to row to this side and also to that side.

The oars of the boat are like a person's tongue: the oars are flat, and the tongue is also flat! To say good or bad, one only needs to use this three-inch red oar.

The Matter of Mr. Fang Weiyi 185

— Wang Sumin

Fang Huan. Zi Weiyi. When his father, Yunting Gong, gave birth to Mr.

He was named Fang Zhong. He was given the surname Zhang. And he was nicknamed Huan. In middle age. He was very famous for his writing. In the two examinations of the Sui and Ke. The Xue Zheng arrived at the academy. He gathered the Xiu Shi from the nine counties of the Su area. He tested the ancient classics in one field. Mr.'s poems, lyrics, ancient Fu, were uniquely the best of the time. Almost no one in the entire area could compete with him. He went to the autumn examination many times. All were unsuccessful. In Ding You. He was selected for the first test. He entered the third test. He was plagued by dysentery. He was unable to complete the test. Therefore, he was dismissed. In Ding Wei. Mr. took office as the head of the land purchasing office for the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, which was run by merchants. He changed his surname to Fang. He used the nickname Huan as his name. He then devoted himself to national affairs. He served as a member of the Provincial Assembly. He was also elected as a member of the Zizhengyuan (National Assembly). After the restoration of the Republic of China. He was appointed as the magistrate of Kunshan. He was courteous to the talented and humble. However, Zhao Kuo understood military affairs on paper. Chen Yu was a general. Yet he had not escaped his nature as a scholar. After acting as the magistrate for a year. He knew that he was not suited to be an official. He strongly recommended Song Chengjia of Yingzhou to be the magistrate. He retired bravely. It was rare and commendable. During the Qi-Lu War. The entire county was restless. Through Mr.'s best efforts to coordinate. It was safe after danger. The national army put down the rebellion. Nanjing was established as the capital. Mr. started again as the secretary of the Ministry of Communications. He retired due to old age. He lived in seclusion in his hometown. The Shanghai Incident suddenly broke out. Mr. discussed national affairs with Mr. Zhang Yifan, a gentry in Jiangsu. He went to Beijing to petition. He died of a minor illness. Alas. Tiger was born late. He met Mr. after the Wuxu year of the Guangxu reign. Mr.'s writing. He did not revise it. And his talent was overflowing. Like an angry horse going down a steep slope. His poetic talent was also like that. Z Jian's seven steps. Fei Qing's eight forks. It was enough to compare. Now Mr. is dead. Death is a common thing. It is a pity that the national studies are about to be extinct. And the spiritual light of the Lu Temple has been destroyed. The articles handed down to the world are unique and eternal. How can one not be sad. Mr. married Wang. He had two sons. Yue Heng Yue Jian. One daughter Yue Qing. She married Chen. Mr. was born on a certain day of a certain month in the Tongzhi reign. He died on a certain day of a certain month in the 21st year of the Republic of China. He lived to be sixty □ years old. According to Mr.'s deeds. There is not much to see. Here is a record of his major deeds. The eulogy says: One who worries about the world before the world worries. One who enjoys the world after the world enjoys. He can rule the world. What the people like, like it. What the people hate, hate it. What one desires to gather. What one hates, do not impose it. He can rule a city. He has neither virtue nor talent. He is only obsessed with fame and wealth. He perseveres. To be trapped in the inextricable. This is a sinner of the world. Mr. knew that being an official was impossible. He decided to give it up. To preserve his truth. He can also be immortal. (Returned Reward)

A Record of Jiangyin Pearl Luo Undershirts 186

— Hongliu

Jiangyin Pearl Luo undershirts. Are a recent product. Its sales

until now. Is less than ten years. Now it is popular in the Suzhou and Changzhou areas. Sales are increasing daily. Not only is it a small industry in our hometown. And it seems to occupy an important position in domestic goods. However, although there are many users in Shanghai. But few know its origin. I will write a few words urgently. As an introduction. It is also an advocacy of domestic goods. According to Jiangyin Pearl Luo undershirts. It is made of square Luo gauze. This Luo gauze. Was originally invented by the Feng family in our hometown. At first, there was no sale on the market. Later, I tried to tailor an undershirt. Buyers came in droves. Therefore, I engaged in large-scale weaving. The cost is also gradually reduced. In the beginning, the best ones cost one yuan and two or three cents each. Now six or seven cents is enough. Buyers think it is cheap. And it is woven with fine threads. The degree of firmness. It can actually match the brocade undershirt. And the value is only one-third of it. The style is a front placket. It is also very convenient to wear. Therefore, everyone is rushing to it. Jiangyin Pearl Luo undershirts. Therefore, it suddenly jumped to the market. At first, only the Feng family sold it exclusively. Two or three years later. It suddenly increased to three or four families. Now it sells in the Suzhou and Changzhou areas. It can be hundreds of thousands of pieces a year. The progress cannot be said to be fast. Unfortunately, few distant places know about this undershirt. It has not been able to be sold throughout the country for a while. Therefore, Yu Le will introduce it. I hope that the people of the country will rise up and promote it together. If there are large capitalists willing to invest in this business. Then its future. It must be even more promising. Now I will tell a story about undershirts. To end my article. Years ago. A tailor from Jiangyin. Knowing that there was no sale of this undershirt in the new capital. Therefore, I bought hundreds of pieces alone. Bundle it up and load it into Beijing. I hope to make a lot of profit. After entering Beijing, it rained for days. The undershirt was half soaked. Also, because Beijing did not know this thing. There were few buyers. And the capital was exhausted. Living in a hotel. There is no way to plan. Day. Passing through the market. It rained. Stand under the eaves of a shop to avoid the rain. The owner of the shop asked what he was selling. Said. Jiangyin undershirt also. The owner had never heard of it before. Please unpack it to watch. And ask how much it costs. Said. The clothes are half soaked. Willing to sell at a reduced price. The owner of the shop said. If so. I will buy it all. Someone was overjoyed. He immediately organized his clothes. How much is soaked. How much is the discount. The rest is as priced. After the delivery is set. Someone thanked him again and again. The owner of the shop then reorganized the purchased undershirts one by one. Then sell it. Buyers

Crowded. Profit doubles. He went to Jiangyin. I took all the things and left. Two or three times in total. He made a lot of money that year. And on the road to Lingling. Therefore, there is also the so-called Jiangyin undershirt. We are from this thing. We can also see Jiangyin undershirts. It can definitely be popular.

An Island That Uses Stones Instead of Currency 189

— Special

Yap Island. Is one of the Caroline Islands located a few degrees north of the equator. After the European War. Entrusted by the League of Nations to Japan for trusteeship. The islanders are brave and fierce. Its tattooed body. Scars. It's scary to look at. The Caroline Islands. It is composed of coral fossils or basalt. And its 400 miles west. There is Barro Island. It is a volcanic fossil. In the past, someone drove a canoe to the island. Take the stone home. Everyone saw that its color was different from the ones produced on this island. I think it's strange. What era was this in? No way to test. The natives of Yap Island have always traded in goods. There are still many places that follow this custom. After the strange stone of Barro Island was transported here. Demand is increasing. This stone has no pleasing color. It cannot be used to make decorative utensils. I don't know why the islanders love

If so. Later, someone exchanged goods for stones. Over time. It has become a standard for transactions. And become a kind of currency. At first, the miners mostly belonged to crushed stones. Later, the more mining, the bigger it became. In recent years, the stones that have been transported here. Some are as big as millstones or wheels. And the thickness is different. So the more expensive its size and weight. It is possible to avoid the thief from running away with it. The stones are all chiseled into a flat shape. There is a hole in the middle. String with rough bamboo. Two people hold its ends. From the stone mine turntable to the beach. Shi Ju. The canoe cannot win. It is tied to a bamboo raft. Dragged for 400 miles. And to Yap. So it can be used for trade. The reason why the islanders use it as currency. Not because the stone is precious. Especially because it is not easy to mine and transport. Stone pickers often encounter wind boat capsizes. Or drowning in the turbulent waves. Or buried in the belly of the fish. Sometimes the bamboo raft sinks. Or because the stone is heavy and difficult to drag. Broken and discarded. It took months to leave home. Experienced all the hardships. Return empty-handed. Desperate. However, there are wise men. Think of a clever way. To comfort these people. If the stone picker can prove that he did go out by boat. Mining Barro. Transported to the beach. Lost in the middle. Then although the person did not bring the stone

Return. But everyone still thinks that he enjoys the lost stone. Like depositing money in a bank. The lost one. Only useless material things. And his hard work to get the stone. Still exists. Because the value of the stone. It also comes from hard work. Simply put. That is to recognize his wealth obtained through hard work and courage. And because of the catastrophe. Did not enjoy it. This recognition. Subject to the island chief. There is no written evidence. Only relying on oral transmission. Since generational succession. As if it were a real product. Anyone with a stone or the right to enjoy the lost stone. And you can transfer it. It also depends on the island chief to remember it in his mind. Recently, the Japanese once imported coins into Yap. Add

There are steamships traveling between Yap and Barro every month. It takes less than two days. Therefore, the currency problem of Yap. Therefore, it has changed. Although coins are convenient. The islanders are very reluctant to use them. Now except for dealings with the government. He followed the old habit of bartering. Although Barro has no stones transported to Yap. But the natives outside. There are still stones of various sizes from time to time. Leaning on the front side. And there are still stones as currency. The Japanese trusteeship government once implemented laws. All contracts. Must go to

Official registration. I heard that an island chief recently inherited the right to enjoy the lost stone through generations. Give it to his married daughter. I followed the law to register with the government for credit. Before long. The new couple used this fictitious stone to buy a coconut plantation. Re-register with the government for transfer. Islanders in small trade. Still use shells from the New Guinea Islands as currency. And have a fixed value. The shells are different from the stones. The color is lovely. And can be used to make decorations. The one who loses the shell. You can't enjoy the virtual right like losing the stone. It is also to avoid red tape.
